      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Mata, tu'kan pɨ' rɨ sa'ne ɨusewankama,</li>
      <li>e'tane tikin nan nɨ esi i'se e'nɨto'. Meri uya nin wakʉ kuru anʉnsa' mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan emo'kato' oton pen ipiyapai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises esi'pʉ ɨpʉreman pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan e'nonkasa' a'tai, tikin nan ipoitorʉ uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ina Epuru, ɨpʉreman eseru pɨ' ina enupakɨ, Isaan uya tʉpoitorʉ ton enupa'pʉ kasa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨwɨpʉrema kon a'tai, se kasa mʉkatʉi': “‘Papai, tʉnamasen pe ɨyese' nesii. Ina esa' pe ɨwe'to' nʉyepʉi.</li>
      <li>Wʉi kaisa rɨ ina irepakɨ wʉi kaisa rɨ te'sen ina i'kiyari ke.</li>
      <li>Ina makooi pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ, apʉne pʉra ina nɨrɨ usentu'ma pɨ' ina pɨ' imakoitasa' kon pɨ'. Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ina kʉsarɨi i'tupɨ'nɨto' ya'.’”</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Iya'tai pʉra tʉtonpa ke ɨwesi a'tai, anomʉra' a'tai ɨutɨ itiwʉ' ta'. Ta auya ipɨ', ‘Osorʉwau pʉreti ke urepa',</li>
      <li>apʉne pʉra utonpa pe te'sen uye'sa', e'tane inta'napato' uya ike pʉra iyesi.’</li>
      <li>Ɨutɨ tawon uya si amaimu eikʉ, ‘Uyanpokʉmai, mʉra'ta uta'kopɨ'ka'sa', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ umunkɨ amʉ' e'nʉnsa' nɨrɨ. Ɨrepase'na e'mʉ'sa'ka poken pʉra man,’ ta iya yau.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya etatɨ', tʉtonpa pe ɨwesi pɨ' ɨrepase'na iye'mʉ'sa'ka pen e'tane, ɨyepiyɨtʉ pʉra ekama'popɨtʉ auya pɨ' ɨrepase'na iye'mʉ'sa'ka i'se ɨwe'to' ke.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ' ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon: Ekama'potɨ', mɨrɨ a'tai ɨyena'nokon nɨ iye'tʉrʉ; iwarinpatɨ', mɨrɨ a'tai eporo auya'nokon; mʉra'ta iwɨpɨ'tɨ', mɨrɨpan uta'kokato' pe ɨyena'nokon.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tanporon kon ekama'po pɨ' na'ne' nan uya eporo; kʉrɨ iwarinpa pɨ' na'ne' uya rɨ eporo; mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kʉrɨ iwɨpɨtʉ pɨ' na'ne' ena' rɨ mʉra'ta uta'koka.</li>
      <li>Nai kʉrɨ warai ikʉipʉnʉ ton uya ɨmu uya moro' pɨ' ɨyekama'po yau, e'tane irepa ɨkʉi ke?</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, mɨnɨ' ke rɨ katɨ irepa iya kɨrɨtɨkɨ pʉmooi ekama'po tane iya?</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nin si ɨri ton uya i'tu yau wakʉ ton e'repan nɨto' ike ke ɨmunkɨ kon repa auya'nokon, mɨrɨ entai kuru ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon, Epʉn pon uya Wakʉ A'kwarʉ tʉrʉ kamoro ekama'ponin nan ena',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises esi'pʉ ɨri a'kwarʉ enpa'ka pɨ' tʉusauro'sen pen ka'pon apai. Ɨri a'kwarʉ epa'ka'pʉ a'tai, tʉusauro'sen pe iyena'pʉ. Mɨrɨ pɨ' ka'pon amʉ' usewansiuka'pʉ</li>
      <li>e'tane, tʉron kon uya ta'pʉ, “Pirɨsipupʉ, makoi amʉ' epuru winɨ makoi amʉ' enpa'kapɨtʉ iya mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon uya i'tupɨtʉ'pʉ tekama'popɨ'se i'tuto' Epʉn winon ku'to' pe iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' usenuminkato' i'tusa' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ti'tui' pʉra rɨ esa' wannɨ pe te'san epantakapɨ'sa' ɨsewa'nomai' uma'ta rɨ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tiwʉ' tawon kon epantakapɨ'sa' ɨsewa'nomai' rɨ uta'mo'ka mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Se'tan epantakapɨtʉ pe iyesi yau tʉpokon pe rɨ ɨsewa'nomai', nai kasa esa' wannɨ pe iye'to' esi moro? Serɨ ta uya apʉne pʉra makoi a'kwarʉ ton enpa'kapɨtʉ uya Pirɨsipupʉ winɨ tukai' ɨye'kupʉ kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ si makoi amʉ' enpa'ka uya pe iyesi yau Pirɨsipupʉ winɨ, ɨnʉ' winɨ ken si ɨpɨkɨron kon uya to' enpa'ka? Mɨrɨ wenai si ɨyeseru kon aimenkanin pe to' esi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane, makoi amʉ' enpa'ka uya pe iyesi yau Papa meruntɨrʉ ke, mɨrɨ nin si Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe uye'sa' ɨpiya'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ nin si Sises esi'pʉ to' enupa pɨ', “Pana'pan ka'pon esi a'tai tepaai ton ke esii'ma tiwʉ' erasu pe, itapuruui ton esi mɨrɨ wakʉ pe rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane, itentaino pana'pan ka'pon uye'sa' a'tai, itentai iyena mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan uya itamataai ton inapurɨnʉ pe te'sen mo'ka, mɨrɨpan uya itapuruui ton tʉneporo'pʉ pantakapɨtʉ tʉtonpa ton ena'.</li>
      <li>“Kʉrɨ uya'kɨrɨ pʉra na'ne' esi uyewa'noma pɨ', kʉrɨ rɨ upokon pe amʉranʉkʉ iya pʉra na'ne' uya ai'pika.</li>
      <li>“Ɨri a'kwarʉ epa'kasa' a'tai ka'pon apai, itɨ siya rɨ a'mun pata yau tereutato' yau warinpa pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan eporo iya pʉra iyesi, mɨrɨ a'tai, ‘Enna'po serɨ ɨutɨ unnɨmɨ'pʉ ta',’ ta iya.</li>
      <li>Iye'sa' a'tai, ɨutɨ eporo iya wakʉ pe akorokasa' pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ikonekasa' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, itɨ 7 kaisaron kon ɨri ton kuru tentaino kon nepʉ iya. To' ewomʉ mɨrɨ yau ɨko'manse'na. Mɨrɨ a'tai, ipan pe, ɨri pe ka'pon esi wapiya tesi'pʉ entai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises usaurokʉ koro'tau, uri'san uya ta'pʉ anpisin koro'tapai, “Pori' pe kuru asan man ɨpɨ'!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Mɨrɨ entai kuru kamoro Papa Maimu etanin nan, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ apurɨnin nan esi mɨrɨ pori' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' epirikʉ koro'tau, Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨri ton nɨ serɨ a'taino kon! Eke Papa tʉrawasooi i'tuto' ipɨkɨrɨ ekama'ponin nan e'tane, ikupʉ uya pen. Isona pɨ', i'tuto' ipɨkɨrɨ rʉ'pʉ rɨken kupʉ uya.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Isona esi'pʉ i'tuto' ipɨkɨrɨ pe Ninipa pon kon pona, mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ Ka'pon, Papa winon esi mɨrɨ serɨ a'taino kon pona.</li>
      <li>Kwin, wʉi enu uye'to' kamisi winon e'mʉ'sa'kato' oton eseru aimenka weyu a'tai serɨ a'taino kon pokon pe to' eno'ma pe; apʉne pʉra iye'sa' wenai non u'matʉ apai Saraman pu'ketʉ etase'na. Serɨ pe eke Saraman entaino man serɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' Ninipa pon kon e'mʉ'sa'kato' oton eseru aimenka weyu a'tai serɨ a'taino kon pokon pe to' eno'ma pe; apʉne pʉra to' era'tɨ'pʉ tʉmakooi kon apai Isona uya itekare ekama pɨ'. Serɨ pe eke Isona entaino man serɨ yau.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ raan'pu po'tɨ pʉra iyesi onansa' pe iye'to' ya' itʉto' pe tʉuya, mɨrɨ pe pʉra pʉsau o'koi'. E'tane ru'ku, itapon pona itʉrʉ iya kamo tewonsan uya iweyu ene poken.</li>
      <li>Ɨyenu kon esi ɨpun kon raan'puui pe. Wakʉ pe ɨyenu kon esi a'tai, tanporo ɨpun kon esi a'kwa pe. E'tane ɨri pe iyesi a'tai, ɨpun kon nɨ nɨrɨ esi ewarupɨ pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ' tense, ka'pon e'to'ka'nʉ'to' pe iyesi wakʉ pe pe' tesi tukai', ɨri pe katɨ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe te'sen to'ka'nʉ'sa' ka'pon uya a'tai, ɨri kupʉ iya pen. Mɨrɨ na'ne' kasa nin si, wakʉ pe ɨnkupʉnʉ kon, weyu uya ɨwei'tɨ kon kasa rɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises usaurokʉ e'nonka tʉpo, tikin nan Pari'si uya ikɨ'ma'pʉ ata're'tɨi'. Mɨrɨpan ewomʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ena'pʉ tʉteire' po tepʉrʉ piyau.</li>
      <li>E'tane Pari'si usewansiuka'pʉ, apʉne pʉra temiyatʉ korʉkasa' Sises uya pʉra iyesi pɨ' tʉuta're'tɨ wapiya, teseru kon yau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Itepuru uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon Pari'si amʉ' uya a'sawʉ kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ aparapii kon korʉka iya'poi pɨ' rɨken, e'tane iyau eke pe rɨ mentai e'nɨto' ɨri pe e'nɨto' esi ayau'nokon.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon iya'kwarʉ pʉnon ka'pon amʉ'! Kʉrɨ pe' iya'poi pɨ' ika'nin nʉ'pʉ uya rɨ marɨ pe' iyawon kapʉ pen?</li>
      <li>E'tane nin aparapii kon yawon itʉtɨ' entu'manin nan ena', mɨrɨpan tanporon nɨ nin si esi mɨrɨ wakʉ pe ɨiwano' kon pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, Pari'si amʉ', apʉne pʉra Papa ena' 1 10 kaisa rɨ min, ru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ti'tui' pʉra rɨ amainarʉ kon yawon ɨi'kiyari kon isu tʉrʉ auya'nokon, e'tane ɨsi'kaisa rɨ ka'pon ku'to' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Papa uya i'nʉnkan nɨto' eno'ma auya'nokon. Emen iwa pe na'ne' kupʉ pɨ' ɨwesi'pʉ kon nesii'no iwapiyaro' tʉnonkai' pʉra ikupʉ pʉra.</li>
      <li>“Papa uya ɨkota'ma kon mɨrɨ ipan pe rɨ, Pari'si amʉ', apʉne pʉra eke ton apon po ɨyereutapɨ'pɨtʉ kon i'nʉnka auya'nokon pɨ' Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' uya, ‘Miyarɨ,’ ta i'se ɨwesi kon ɨpɨ'nokon kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' e'nɨ pata'se' yau.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, apʉne pʉra ima'kʉmasa' pen uruwai' kasa ɨwesi kon, ka'pon amʉ' usato' ipʉro'poro i'tui'ma pʉra,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Main pɨ' enupanin nan tonpa uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ti'sa, serɨ tasa' auya a'tai, ina piyɨ'nʉ'pɨ'pɨtʉ auya,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, Main pɨ' enupanin nan, Papa uya ɨkota'ma kon mɨrɨ ipan pe, apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' apiyo'masa' auya'nokon sa'man nɨ ku'to' pe to' uya Papa Maimu serɨ tukai', mɨrɨpan kon pika'tɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi ikupʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, apʉne pʉra pu'kena' amʉ' uruwasii oton tɨ' akapɨtʉ'pʉ auya'nokon, mɨrɨpan atamokori kon amʉ' uya to' tʉ'ka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ɨusekama kon atamokori kon nʉkupʉ'pʉ pɨ' i'napairon ta auya'nokon; pu'kena' amʉ' tʉ'ka'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan to' uruwasii oton tɨ' akapɨtʉ'pʉ auya'nokon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, pena rɨ Papa uya tʉpu'ketʉ yau ta'pʉ, ‘Pu'kena' amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itekare ekamanin nan ennoko uya mɨrɨ. Tʉron kon tʉ'kato' oton to' uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon kota'mato' oton to' uya.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', serɨ a'taino kon e'to' oton pu'kena' amʉ' mʉnʉ esa' pe itɨsa' rʉ'pʉ orʉ epiya'tɨ'pʉ si'kɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>Eperʉ mʉnʉ awonsi'kɨ Sakaraya mʉnʉ pʉ'kʉ pona iwɨsa' rʉ'pʉ Papa ena' use'man nɨto' apon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' ka'sanau. Ewai', ekama uya, serɨ a'taino kon e'to' oton tanporo serɨ esa' pe.</li>
      <li>“Ɨsɨ sɨ, ipan pe main i'tunin nan, apʉne pʉra i'tunin pe e'nɨto' kii mo'kasa' auya'nokon pɨ'. Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨ epa'kasa' pʉra iyesi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tepa'kasan wa'kʉ'pɨtʉ auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, Pari'si pata'se' apai Sises enna'po'pʉ. Mɨrɨ si'kɨrɨ rɨ, Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan ena'pʉ iteyaton pe. Mɨrɨpan ekama'popɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya sa'man ton pɨ' rɨ,</li>
      <li>a'sito' tʉuya'nokon ipɨkɨrɨ oton nɨ imaimu eta i'se to' esi'pʉ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mɨrɨ koro'tau, anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' amʉra'pʉ. Tu'ke ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ, tʉtonpa kon nɨ tʉwasa'pɨ'se. Wapiya tʉpoitorʉ ton auro'kapɨ' Sises e'sara'tɨ'pʉ: “Te'mainanpai' e'tɨ', Pari'si amʉ' uya pʉrowa a'sarutanʉ'to' ike namai', wakʉ pe to' e'ku'to'.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ iwapu'tɨsa' te'nɨponkasen pen, mɨrɨ pe pʉra onansa' i'tu pʉra te'sen.</li>
      <li>Ewarupɨ yau ausaurokʉ'pʉ usetato' oton wʉi nai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pana ya' ɨyetarerumʉ'pʉ i'nau ɨiwʉ' tau usekamato' oton ɨutɨ nakapu ponsi'kɨ.</li>
      <li>“Apana'tɨ uya 'nokon, utonpa ton, ɨpun kon wɨnin nan pɨ' kenari'nʉntʉu, mɨrɨ tʉpo ɨ'rɨ kupʉ to' uya pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>E'tane ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon kʉrɨ rɨ ɨyenari'nʉnto' kon ipɨ'. Kʉrɨ rɨ pɨ' rɨken enari'nʉntɨ', ama'tanʉkʉ tʉpo, a'kwarʉ wannɨ kuru rɨ eno'manin kʉrɨ rɨ, ekota'man nɨto' ya'. Ewai', apana'tɨ uya 'nokon, kʉrɨ rɨ rɨken pɨ' enari'nʉntɨ'.</li>
      <li>“5 kaisaron kon pe' toron amʉ' tʉkʉrʉpo'pomasan pen asa'ron pʉrata pun kaisa rɨ? E'tane tikin nan nɨ to' tonpa pu'tɨka'nʉkʉ Papa uya pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>I'napai rɨ, a'pai kon i'po' rɨ esi tanporo i'tusa' pe. Kenari'nʉntʉu, i'nʉnkena' ton ɨmɨrɨ'nokon tu'kan kon toron amʉ' entaino kon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Apana'tɨ uya 'nokon, ɨnʉ' uya rɨ uyekama a'tai, i'nai rɨ iyesi tukai' ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', Ka'pon, Papa winon uya ekamato' oton i'nai rɨ iyesi tukai' Papa inserʉʉi ton pɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ unurunpayai'ne' ka'pon amʉ' rau nurunpato' oton Papa inserʉʉi ton rau.</li>
      <li>“Tanporon kon tʉusauro'san isapema pe Ka'pon, Papa winon pɨ' rɨ usentu'man, e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉusauro'sen esi a'tai, Wakʉ A'kwarʉ sapema pe pɨ', Papa usentu'man pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>“Usenupan nɨto' iwʉ', esa' wannɨ ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke ton rakʉi' to' uya ɨne'sa' kon a'tai, kɨsewankamatʉu, nai kasa e'wapu'tɨ mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨ'rɨ ta uya, tukai'.</li>
      <li>Papa A'kwarʉ uya amaimu ke ɨrepa mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ a'tai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' koro'tawon uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ti'sa, urui pɨ' ekamakɨ urepato' pe iya a'sa'mʉyai ina kʉipʉnʉ apuruui rʉ'pʉ ke,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Utʉrawasooi pen nɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, ta'pʉ iya tu'kan kon pɨ', “Ti'tui' e'tɨ'! Mentai pʉra e'tɨ'! Ka'pon uko'mamʉ pʉra rɨ iyesi serɨ non po inke pori' pe tanporon esa' pe tesi pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya panton ke to' auro'ka'pʉ to' enupanin pe, “Tapiyara ka'pon esi'pʉ, eke imainarʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan usenuminka'pʉ, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kupʉ uya serɨ?’ tukai'. ‘Ui'kiyari amʉranʉ'to' uya ya' pʉra iyesi.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai ta'pʉ iya, ‘Serɨ kupʉ uya; uyapuruui iwʉ' tʉrʉ'kwa uya serɨ. Eke pe parɨ amɨto' pe uya. Mɨrɨ yau si ui'kiyari mɨrɨ tʉpo uyapuruui amʉranʉ'to' pe uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si ta uya mɨrɨ, Tu'kan nɨ amʉranʉ'sa' uya mɨrɨ uko'manʉ'nin pe. E'tʉrawasoma pen nin si serɨ tʉpo. Enta'na, ensi uya, pori' pe uko'mamʉ!’</li>
      <li>“E'tane, Papa uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', ‘Pu' pʉn! Serɨ ewarupɨ nau auma'tato' oton. E'tane si tiwano' pe, ɨiwano' pe ɨnkupʉ'pʉ epoto' oton tʉron nɨ uya,’ ta'pʉ Papa uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ na'ne' kasa si te'ton kon ka'pon amʉ' mentaino kon pe to' esi a'tai, apʉne pʉra Papa e'to' i'se kupʉ to' uya pʉra iyesi pɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ' ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨuko'manto' kon pɨ' rɨ kɨsewankamatʉu, ɨ'rɨ pɨ' enta'nato' pe, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨpun kon pɨ' rɨ, ɨ'rɨ esi upon pe, tukai'.</li>
      <li>Uko'man nɨto' esi kiyari entai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pun wannɨ, pon entai.</li>
      <li>Toron amʉ' pɨ' ɨsenupatɨ': Te'pɨnsan pen, kiyari akʉ'pʉsa' amʉranʉ'nin nan pen, to' i'kiyari pata'se' pʉnon kon nɨ; e'tane Papa uya to' ewekʉ. Mɨrɨ entai i'nʉnkena' pe ɨwesi kon mɨrɨ toron amʉ' entai!</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ tʉuko'manto' ɨnka miyarɨ parɨ, ipɨ' tʉusewankamai'?</li>
      <li>Sepa' nan kupʉ auya'nokon poken pʉra iye'tane, ɨ'rɨ pɨ' ken si tʉron nɨ ton pɨ' ɨusewankama kon?</li>
      <li>“Pata ipʉrʉ ton a'ta pɨ' ɨsenupatɨ': Te'tʉrawasomasan pen, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨ'pɨ'nin nan pen. Mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane, ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ'nokon, Saraman imaminkena' epontɨsa' pʉra iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ ton kasa.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa Papa uya wana' rɨ pontɨ pe iyesi yau, wana' serɨ pe na'ne' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ awanapairɨ eno'ma apo' ya', mɨrɨ entai rɨ ɨpontɨ iya 'nokon. Aiko sɨ, aiko pe rʉ'kwɨ apurɨto' auya'nokon esi!</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyewan kon tʉnonkai' pʉra e'tɨ' ɨnɨkunʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnensinʉ kon pɨ'; ipɨ' kɨsewankamatʉu.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra Papa i'tunin nan pen e'to' ipɨkɨrɨ pe tanporo serɨ warai'nan esi, mɨrɨpan ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon uya i'tu serɨ ton i'se ɨwesi kon.</li>
      <li>E'tane, esa' wannɨ pe iye'to' iwarinpatɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ serɨ ton nɨ nin si e'tʉrʉ mɨrɨ ɨyena'nokon nɨ nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Tu'ke pʉra rɨ esii'ma, enari'ke' pe pʉra e'tɨ', apʉne pʉra ɨkʉipʉnʉ kon man pori' pe itesa' pe rɨ marɨ ɨwesi kon pa ɨrepa kon tʉuya pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ayapuruui kon ikʉrʉpo'pomatɨ', entu'manin nan repa kon pa. Ɨpʉrataai kon yen ɨnepotɨ' ipooi'pɨ pe tenasen pen, mamin, Epʉn po na'ne' tʉu'ma'sen pen. Mɨrɨ yau ama' uyepʉ pʉra iyesi a'ko pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨrʉkanin uya ima'tanʉkʉ pʉra rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra, ɨimamin kon e'to' airɨ, mɨrɨ yau ɨyewan kon nɨ nɨrɨ e'to' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ to' enupa'pʉ iya se kasa, “Iyekonekasa' pe e'tɨ', Papa tʉrawasooi ku'nin pe inke rɨ.</li>
      <li>Iyapiyo' ton esi tepuru kon enupɨkɨrɨ kasa e'tɨ'. Iye'sa' a'tai, mʉra'ta wɨpɨtʉ iya a'tai, inke pʉra to' uya a'koka iyewonto' pe.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe to' esi mɨrɨ itenupɨkɨrɨ te'san. I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, iyepontɨ mɨrɨ to' mʉta'napato' pe tʉuya, tepʉrʉ piyau tʉteire' kon po to' enato' pe to' kupʉ iya, mɨrɨpan kon enta'na enupɨkɨrɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe kuru iyesi mɨrɨ kamoro iyapiyo' ton itenupɨkɨrɨ te'san, ɨ'rɨ pe pʉra rɨ ewarupɨ nau rɨ iye'tane.</li>
      <li>E'tane, se ito'ka'nʉ'tɨ': Ɨutɨ esa' uya ama' uyepʉ i'tusa' yau, tiwʉ' ta' ewon nɨ kuu'pʉ iya nesii'no pen.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨrɨ, tekonekai' me'tʉi', apʉne pʉra Ka'pon, Papa winon uye'to' oton itenupɨkɨrɨ pʉra rɨ ɨwe'tane'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ, “Uyepuru, ina rɨken pe' pana ya' serɨ panton ekama auya, mɨrɨ pe pʉra tanporon kon pɨ' rɨ katɨ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Itepuru uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' ken usauro'nɨ'pʉ awɨron mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ emiya'pokena' tʉtonpa esa' e' pe nai? Itesa' nʉnonkanʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton esa' pe to' i'kiyari epe' ke to' repanin pe itʉto' weyu a'tai?</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ e'to' oton itepuru neporonʉ mɨrɨ kupʉ pɨ' tenna'po a'tai.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, itepuru uya tanporon tapuruui esa' pe iku'to' oton.</li>
      <li>E'tane si iya'tai pʉra kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ uya ta pe iyesi yau, ‘Uyepuru nʉko'manyan inke rɨ, iyepʉ pʉra,’ ta iya yau, mɨrɨpan e'sara'tɨ warawo' amʉ', uri'sami'si amʉ' ipoitorʉ ton panta'ma pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ enta'nan pɨ', ensi pɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ e'taripan pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ epuru uye'to' oton wʉi a'tai itenupɨkɨrɨ iye'tane pʉra, mɨrɨ a'kʉra' iyepʉ ta tane iya pʉra rɨ, mɨrɨpan uya ipɨrʉkato' oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ inonkato' iya oton apurɨnin nan pen pata'se' ya'.</li>
      <li>“Kʉrɨ rɨ ipoitorʉ epuru e'to' i'se i'tunin e'tane tekonekasen pen, tepuru tʉrawasooi ku'nin pen nɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kota'mato' oton itepuru uya ipan pe kuru.</li>
      <li>E'tane kʉrɨ rɨ i'tunin pen tepuru e'to' i'se, mɨrɨpan uya ɨri kupʉ, mara rʉ'kwɨ itepuru uya ikota'mato' oton. Kʉrɨ rɨ eke pe Papa uya irepasa' na'ne' winɨ eke pe iwarinpa iya. Kʉrɨ rɨ nɨrɨ Papa uya irepasa' na'ne' itemiya'porʉ ke, eke pe kuru tʉrawaso ku'to' iya ike ke winɨ, ekama'poto' oton eke pe kuru itʉrawasooi rʉ'pʉ pɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ marɨ Sises esi'pʉ to' enupa pɨ' se kasa: “Apo' ne'sa' uya serɨ non pona, epo'tɨn pɨ' iye'sara'tɨka'sa' i'se e'ai'.</li>
      <li>Uma'tanʉ'to' ya' utɨ pe man, e'tane e'ne' pe kuru ukupʉ iya serɨ iu'matʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Tʉusewankamai' pʉra pe' e'nɨto' ne'sa' uya pe ekama auya'nokon serɨ non pona? Tʉusewankamai' pʉra e'nɨto' ne'sa' uya pen, e'tane epantakapɨ'nɨto' nin.</li>
      <li>Serɨ awonsi'kɨ, 5 kaisaron kon ka'pon amʉ' e'to' oton ɨsitonpa pe usewa'noman pɨ'; osorʉwawon kon asa'ron kon ewa'noma pɨ', asa'ron kon osorʉwawon kon ewa'noma pɨ' nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>To' epantakapɨ'sa' e'to' oton; ikʉipʉnʉ tʉmu ewa'noma pɨ', imu tʉkʉipʉnʉ ewa'noma pɨ', isan uri'san tʉmʉre ewa'noma pɨ', imʉre uri'san tʉsan ewa'noma pɨ', itewo'pʉ tʉpa'se ewa'noma pɨ', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipa'se tewo'pʉ ewa'noma pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Kapuru' enuku ene auya'nokon a'tai, wʉi enu utɨ winɨ, inke pʉra, tuna uyepʉ tukai' i'tu auya'nokon, mɨrɨ koro'tau iye'kapʉ rɨ.</li>
      <li>Wʉi enu enuku kamisi winɨ pese'tɨ uyepʉ a'tai, i'tu auya'nokon, a'ne' pe wʉi uyepʉ tukai', mɨrɨpan esi a'ne' pe rɨ.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe te'ku'san! I'tu auya'nokon non mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka' winɨ rɨ ɨ'rɨ rɨ enpoikanin pe ɨwesi kon. Ɨ'rɨ pe ken si iyesi pɨ' serɨ pe iweyu na'ne' enpoika i'tu auya'nokon pʉra iyesi?</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' wakʉ eseru ɨnto'ka'nʉ'pai pʉra ɨwesi kon ɨiwano' kon pe?</li>
      <li>Ɨutɨ kon koro'tau ɨyeyaton a'kɨrɨ a'sinin itepuru piya', ipan pe ɨsi'tukɨ ekoneka i'se ipokon pe, aya'kwarʉka iya rawɨrɨ a'sinin itepuru ena', ɨtʉrʉ iya mɨrɨ pʉresiman ena', mɨrɨpan uya ɨyeno'ma pariki'si ta'.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya, ɨyepa'kato' oton kon pen nɨ tanporo ɨne'manʉ kon i'ma'ka auya'nokon pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Moron kon uya Sises pana'tɨ'pʉ Kiyarari pon kon pɨ' Paire' nʉsuma'san imʉnʉ pɨ' to' use'mato' pokon pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Serɨ kasa to' uma'tasa' pɨ' ɨri ton pe kuru to' esi'pʉ pe kʉsekamatʉu.</li>
      <li>Kane, ta uya, ɨyera'tɨ kon pʉra iyesi yau amakooi kon apai, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨ nɨrɨ uma'ta mɨrɨ to' kasa rɨ marɨ ɨwesi kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe pʉra 18 kaisaron kon iyeri'sa' kon Sairon pon ka'ta' amɨsa' ɨutɨ uta'mo'kasa' a'tai tʉpona'nokon. Surusiran pon kon entai kuru pe' ɨri pe to' esi'pʉ pe ekama auya'nokon, mɨrɨ wenai to' e'wɨnɨ'pʉ na'ne'?</li>
      <li>Kane, ta uya, ɨyera'tɨ kon pʉra iyesi yau amakooi kon apai, ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨ nɨrɨ uma'ta mɨrɨ to' kasa rɨ marɨ ɨwesi kon pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya se panton ekama'pʉ, “Ka'pon esi'pʉ pi' e' esa'. Mɨrɨpan utɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iteperu ense e'tane, eporo iya pʉra iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya tʉmainarʉ esa' pɨ', ‘Osorʉwau wʉipiya e'to' airɨ utɨpɨ'sa' man ui'kiyari epetasa' ene i'se e'tane, eporo uya pʉra rɨ iye'sa'. A'tɨkɨ! Ɨ'rɨto' pe non iwanʉ'ka iya nesii'no?’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan eikʉ'pʉ imainarʉ esa' uya, ‘Tɨwɨ tikin nɨ rɨken wʉipiya isi'tuka'to' pe nesii. Iwoi aka uya, mɨrɨpan epetanʉ'nin ke iu'na'tɨto' pe uya.</li>
      <li>Iyepetasa' pe iyesi yau, wakʉ pe nin si iyesi mɨrɨ; mɨrɨ pʉra iyesi yau, a'tɨto' pe rɨ nin si,’ ta'pʉ iya,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sapa' a'tai, Sises esi'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan yau uri'san esi'pʉ tɨmuipan, ɨri a'kwarʉ nʉtɨmuika'pʉ 18 kaisa rɨ wʉipiya iko'mansa'. Ipan pe iye'tɨmuikasa' to'sa rɨ iyena pʉra.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ensa' a'tai, ikɨ'ma'pʉ iya tʉpiya'. Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ma'non, ɨyeparan apai ɨmo'ka uya serɨ.”</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, temiyatʉ tʉrʉ'pʉ iya ipona, mɨrɨ a'tai rɨ nin si, to'sa rɨ iyena'pʉ mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan uya Papa apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ka'pon epi'tɨsa' pɨ' Sapa' a'tai, tʉusakorota pe Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' epuru uya ta'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “6 kaisa rɨ moro wʉi esi mɨrɨ e'tʉrawasoman weyu. Mɨrɨ ton weyu a'tai, ɨsepi'tɨi' ɨsi'tɨ', Sapa' a'tai pen,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon wakʉ pe te'ku'san! Sapa' a'tai pe' ɨikʉn kon paka, isa'ka'si rɨ eukanin nan pen ɨmɨrɨ'nokon iten apai tuna ensise'na arɨ kon pa?</li>
      <li>Pʉse rɨ ken pe' si uri'san Epʉra'an pa rʉ'pʉ, Se'tan newa'tɨ'pʉ 18 kaisa rɨ wʉipiya euka pen ken pe' si Sapa' a'tai?” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ta iya a'tai, tanporo iteyaton non ɨpiyɨtʉ'pʉ, e'tane ka'pon amʉ' epori'ma'pʉ tanporon wakʉ ton inkupʉnʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ kasa Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi? Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' mɨrɨ kasa iyesi tukai' ekama uya?</li>
      <li>Mosta' ena'pɨ kasa iyesi, ka'pon nʉpɨmɨnʉ tʉmainarʉ yau. Iya'ta, mɨrɨpan ena eke pe, mɨrɨpan panta po toron amʉ' esi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ekama'pokaa'pʉ iya kanan, “Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' mɨrɨ kasa Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi ta uya?</li>
      <li>Pʉrowa a'sarutanʉ'nin kasa iyesi, uri'san nanʉmʉnʉ, mɨrɨpan uya pʉrowa pokon pe eke pe iki'ma tanporo ipun yau iyena pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises utɨ esi'pʉ eke iwa ton pata awɨrɨ'ne rɨ, Surusiran pona tʉutɨi'ma rɨ, ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Uyepuru, tu'kan kon pen nɨ si ka'pon amʉ' pika'tɨto' oton Papa uya to' ato' pe tʉuya Epʉn pona?” ta'pʉ iya. Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ',</li>
      <li>“Ɨsi'tutɨ' kuru rɨ aiko rʉ'kwɨ mʉra'ta awɨrɨ ewon nɨ pɨ', ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, apʉne pʉra tu'kan kon usi'tuto' oton ewomʉ i'se, e'tane to' ewonto' oton pen.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, ɨutɨ esa' e'mʉ'sa'ka, mɨrɨpan uya mʉra'ta a'koro, pʉroroi po ɨye'soto'kasa' esii'ma mʉra'ta wɨpɨtʉ auya'nokon ipan pe ekama'po pe, ‘Ina epuru, mʉra'ta a'kokakɨ ina iwano' pe,’ mɨrɨ e'tane, ɨyeikʉ iya 'nokon, ‘Ɨi'tu uya 'nokon pʉra man, mɨrɨ pe pʉra mɨrɨ winɨ ɨuye'sa' kon ta uya pʉra rɨ iyesi,’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai nin si, ‘Ɨpokon pe sa'ne ina nʉta're'tɨtai ko, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' menupatai ko ina e'ma tau'ne.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan e'tane, ɨyeikʉ iya 'nokon, ‘Ɨi'tu uya 'nokon pʉra man, mɨrɨ pe pʉra mɨrɨ winon kon uye'sa' ta uya pʉra rɨ iyesi. Entantɨ' upiyapai, tanporo ɨmɨrɨ'nokon ɨri ku'nin nan!’ tato' iya oton.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ yau, ukaran nɨto' oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨ e'kɨtɨtɨi'mato' oton, Epʉra'an, Aisi', Seko' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pu'kena' amʉ' ene auya'nokon a'tai, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau, ɨyeno'masa' kon e'tane.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' uye'to' oton wʉi enu uyepʉ winɨ, wʉi enu utɨ winɨ, wʉi enu enwo'netʉ winɨ, wʉi enu kamisi winɨ, mɨrɨpan kon ereutato' oton enta'nan pɨ' Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau.</li>
      <li>I'napai rɨ, kamoro iu'matʉ pe na'ne' nan wapiya te'ton kon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wapiya na'ne' nan iu'matʉ pe te'ton kon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Pari'si amʉ' uyee'pʉ Sises piya', mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Serɨ apai tʉron nɨ airɨ enta, Era' e'kaman pɨ' man ɨwɨnɨ pɨ',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Kʉrɨ rɨ pata ennakanin ipana'tɨtantɨ' unkupʉnʉ pɨ': ‘Ɨri a'kwarʉ ton enpa'ka pɨ' esi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' epi'tɨ pɨ' esi, serɨ pe, awanapai rɨ nɨrɨ, mɨrɨ ema'sa' yau'ne rɨ nin si utʉrawasooi u'ma'sa' pe iyesi mɨrɨ.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ koro'tau rɨ nin si, utɨ rɨ, serɨ pe, awanapai rɨ, mɨrɨ ema'sa' yau, Surusiran pona. I'napai rɨ iyesi, ɨnʉ' rɨ pu'kena' wɨto' pʉra iyesi mɨrɨ mɨ airɨ rɨ e'tane Surusiran po rɨken.</li>
      <li>“Aiko sɨ, Surusiran pon kon, Surusiran pon kon! Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon, pu'kena' amʉ' tʉ'kanin nʉ'san, ɨpiya'nokon Papa nennoko'san wɨpɨ'nin nʉ'san tɨ' ke. Inke rɨ sa'ne ɨmunkɨ amʉ' amʉranʉkʉ i'se esi'pʉ, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uya tʉmunkɨ amʉranʉkʉ kasa tapiri o'koi', e'tane ikupʉ uya i'se pʉra ɨwesi'pʉ kon.</li>
      <li>Apʉne si entɨ', ɨiwʉ' kon e'nonkasa' ɨyena'nokon yawon pʉra. Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, uyento' auya'nokon oton pen nɨ kanan serɨ enta', ‘Pori' pe rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ nʉye'ai'ne' Itepuru ese' yau esi,’ ta auya'nokon pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sapa' a'tai, Sises utɨ'pʉ Pari'si amʉ' epuru iwʉ' ta' enta'nai'. Ipan pe rɨ to' esi'pʉ enpɨtʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau si, takuru'kenan esi'pʉ mɨrɨ itemekon ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ i'si ton a'sarutapɨ'sa'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan ekama'po'pʉ, “Main awɨrɨ pe' e'nɨ pe iyesi Sapa' a'tai takuru'kenan ka'pon epi'tɨ yau, mɨrɨ pe pʉra kane katɨ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane to' uya rɨ etapɨtʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan uya temiyatʉ tʉrʉ'pʉ takuru'kenan pona, epi'tɨ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan ennoko'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, to' ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Ɨ'rɨ ken kupʉ auya ɨmʉre, mɨrɨ pe pʉra ɨikʉn paka uta'mo'kasa' pe iyesi yau non akasa' ya' Sapa' a'tai? Imo'ka auya pen pe' inke pʉra?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ nin si tato' to' uya pʉra rɨ iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ a'tai, Sises uya ikɨ'masa' kon ereutasa' ene'pʉ eke ton pe te'san apon po. Mɨrɨpan kon pana ya' se panton ekama'pʉ iya:</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨkɨ'masa' pe iyesi yau, temari'masan uta're'tɨ koro'ta', eke ton pata'se' airɨ kereutai. Iya'tai pʉra, eke ɨyentaino kɨ'masa' iya esi.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi yau, apatawono ɨkɨ'manin nʉ'pʉ uya ta ɨpɨ', ‘Pʉse irepakɨ ayapon ke.’ Mɨrɨ a'tai nin si, ɨyepiyɨ'sa' ereuta mɨrɨ sepan pona rʉ'kwɨ nin si.</li>
      <li>E'tane ɨkɨ'masa' a'tai, sepan airɨ rʉ'kwɨ mereutai'. Apatawono uye'sa' a'tai, ‘Se ya' parɨ wakʉ ya' atamakɨ,’ tato' pe iya ɨpɨ'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, eke pe ɨkupʉ iya ɨpokon pe ikɨ'masa' kon enu airɨ.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra, eke pe te'ku'san tiwano' kon pe ena mɨrɨ se pe rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ se pe te'ku'san ena mɨrɨ eke pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpatawono pɨ', “Ɨye'kɨ'ma a'tai, ɨtonpa ton nɨken kʉ'kɨ'mai, tapiyara ton kʉ'kɨ'mai, apʉne pʉra to' use'ma esi ɨmɨrɨ tʉkɨ'mai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane enta'nai' ka'pon amʉ' kɨ'ma auya pe iyesi yau, entu'manin nan, ipu'tɨka'sa' ton, wasesenpa' nan, tenku'na' nan nɨken mʉkɨ'mai'.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe ɨwesi mɨrɨ, to' uya ɨye'ma tane pʉra rɨ. Ɨyepe'pʉ eporo auya, ipokena' ton eri'sa' e'mʉ'sa'ka a'tai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' mɨrɨ yau te'san tonpa uya a'tai, ta'pʉ iya Sises pɨ', “Pori' pe kuru kamoro esi mɨrɨ enta'nan pɨ' te'ton kon Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe yau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ panton ekama pe, “Ka'pon uya eke kuru enta'nan nɨto' koneka esi'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan uya tu'kan kon nɨ ka'pon amʉ' kɨ'ma'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tenta'nakapʉ a'tai nin si, tʉpoitorʉ ennoko'pʉ iya tʉnkɨ'ma'san pana'tɨse'na, ‘Ɨsi'tɨ' si, tanporon nɨ si ekonekasa' man,’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane, tanporo tʉwapu kon eporo'pʉ to' uya. Wapiyaro' uya ta'pʉ, ‘Serɨ pe kuru umɨ ennasa' uya man, mɨrɨpan ense'na utɨ. Ɨri pe mɨrɨ pɨ' ke'kupʉi.’</li>
      <li>“Tʉron nɨ uya ta'pʉ, ‘Serɨ pe kuru 5 kaisa rɨ asa'rɨ'ne i'mʉkansa' kon paka amʉ' waraino kon ennasa' uya man, mɨrɨpan kon i'tuse'na utɨ serɨ. Ɨri pe mɨrɨ pɨ' ke'kupʉi.’</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ uya rɨ marɨ kanan ta'pʉ, ‘Serɨ pe kuru emari'masa' man. Mɨrɨ wenai, utɨ poken pʉra man,’ tukai' to' usekama'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Serɨ si ekamase'na ipoitorʉ enna'po'pʉ mɨrɨ tepuru pɨ'. Mɨrɨ pɨ' itepuru usakorota'pʉ ipan pe, mɨrɨpan uya tʉpoitorʉ apiyo'ma'pʉ, ‘Inke pʉra enta pata ya'ne, eke ton asanta tawɨrɨ'ne, aiko ton tawɨrɨ'ne entu'manin nan ine'ta, ipu'tɨka'sa' kon, tenku'na' nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wasesenpa' nan,’ ta'pʉ itepuru uya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan poitorʉ uye'sa' uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', ‘Uyapiyo'ma'pʉ auya siku'kapʉi, e'tane moro rɨ marɨ ɨutɨ man, iyarʉ pʉra,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai, itepuru uya kanan takaa'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ pɨ', ‘Enta asanta ta'ne ɨnnɨ' nan pata ya'ne mɨrɨ yawon kon pɨ' ɨsi'tɨ' kuru mʉkai', uiwʉ' utarʉ'tɨka'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Ta uya ɨpɨ', kamoro unkɨ'ma'san wapiya uya ui'kiyari onpato' oton pen,’ ta'pʉ itepuru uya tapiyo' pɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Anpisin nɨ utɨ esi'pʉ Sises a'kɨrɨ. To' winɨkʉi' tera'tɨi' ta'pʉ iya,</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' rɨ esi pʉra iyesi upoitorʉ pe tʉkʉipʉnʉ, tʉsan i'nʉnkai'ma, tʉno'pʉ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉmunkɨ amʉ', takon non mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉparusi ton, tʉuko'mamʉ eseru rɨ nɨrɨ i'nʉnkai'ma rɨ urɨ i'nʉnkato' tʉuya entai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉkurusukuui anapai pʉra na'ne' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ upɨkɨrɨ ɨtɨpai pʉra na'ne' esi upoitorʉ poken pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ka'tawon ɨutɨ anamɨpai ɨtonpa kon esi yau, iyereuta pen pe' wapiya eke pe pe' tʉpʉrataai esi amɨ poken nɨ tukai' ense'na?</li>
      <li>Isara'tɨsa' iya e'tane, i'ma'ka iya pʉra iyesi yau, tanporon kon ennin nan uta'kɨrɨ mɨrɨ ipɨ',</li>
      <li>‘Pʉse rɨ rʉ'kwɨ e'sara'tɨ'pʉ amɨ pɨ' e'tane, i'ma'ka iya pʉra iye'sa',’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>“Iya'tai pʉra si, kin ekoneka serɨ ko tʉutɨto' pe tʉron nɨ kin ewa'nomai', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itentai enai'. Iyereuta pen pe' ɨsenuminkase'na 10,000 kaisaron kon tʉsoisaai amʉ' pe' esi pana' pe tukai' teyaton non uyepʉ pe iyesi yau 20,000 kaisa rɨ tewa'nomai'?</li>
      <li>Ikupʉ tʉuya poken pʉra iyesi pɨ', tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko iya kin piya' ɨnnɨ rɨ marɨ esii'ma ekama'pose'na tʉuko'manto' kon pe tʉusewa'nomai' pʉra.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', upoitorʉ pe e'pai ɨwesi yau, tanporon nɨ tʉnonkai' ɨwe'to' pe iyesi.</li>
      <li>“Waiyo esi wakʉ, e'tane ine'ne' pe pʉra iyenasa' yau, nai kasa ine'ne' pe kanan ikupʉ?</li>
      <li>Wakʉ pe pʉra rɨ iyesi non iwano' pe mɨrɨ pe pʉra non isu pe; eno'masa' pe iyesi. “Kʉrɨ tʉpana ke na'ne' etanin pe, tɨwɨ netai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ a'tai, pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉmakooikena' nan amʉra esi'pʉ Sises woi imaimu etase'na.</li>
      <li>E'tane Pari'si amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan etarerumʉ'pʉ, “Pʉse rɨ ka'pon uya tʉmakooikena' nan kupʉ tʉtonpa pe, to' pokon pe rɨ iyenta'na!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai nin si, Sises uya serɨ ton panton amʉ' ekama'pʉ mɨrɨ to' pɨ',</li>
      <li>“Iya'tai pʉra, 100 kaisa rɨ karimeru amʉ' itikʉn ton ɨtonpa kon esi yau, mɨrɨpan kon tonpa utano'masa' pe iyesi yau, 99 pan kon pe' nɨnnin pen ayupon pata yau itano'masa' e'ma'pʉ tau tʉutɨto' pe eporo tʉuya pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ?</li>
      <li>Eposa' tʉuya a'tai, pori' pe esii'ma ti'mʉye'pɨ pona anʉmʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, tʉtonpa ton kɨ'ma iya, mɨrɨpan uya ta to' pɨ', ‘Epori'manpai'nokon. Uikʉn karimeru itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ eposa' uya man!’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, mɨrɨ kasa kuru si iyesi epori'man esi eke pe Epʉn po tikin nan tʉmakooikenan era'tɨsa' a'tai, kamo 99 kaisaron kon ipokena' ton ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' pori' pe e'nɨ entai.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pe pʉra, uri'san uya 10 kaisaron pʉrata pun tonpa ano'ma'pʉ pe iyesi yau tikin nɨ, ɨ'rɨ ken si kupʉ iya? Tʉraan'puui po'tɨ iya, tiwʉ' akorokato' pe tʉuya, iwarinpa iya, eporo tʉuya pʉ'kʉ pona.</li>
      <li>Eposa' tʉuya a'tai, tʉtonpa ton kɨ'ma iya, mɨrɨpan uya ta to' pɨ', ‘Epori'manpai'nokon, itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ upʉrataai eposa' uya man!’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ iyesi ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Papa inserʉʉi amʉ' epori'ma tikin nan nɨ tʉmakooikenan era'tɨsa' a'tai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Miyarɨ rɨ Sises usaurokʉ'pʉ, “Moro ka'pon esi'pʉ asa'ron kon imunkɨ.</li>
      <li>Iyakon uya ta'pʉ tʉkʉipʉnʉ pɨ', ‘Papai, uyena' ɨntʉrʉnʉ pe te'sen ɨimamin itʉka'kɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'. Mɨrɨpan uya timamin ratoika'pʉ to' kaisa rɨ.</li>
      <li>Inke kuru pʉra rɨ mɨrɨ pata'pʉ pe, imu akon si uya tanporo tiwano' pe iye'nonkasa' amʉranʉkʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ ɨnnon pata ya'. Mɨrɨ yau nin si tʉpʉrataai ma'tanʉkʉ'pʉ iya mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Tanporon nɨ nin si ma'tanʉkʉ'pʉ iya pata'pʉ pe, iwankan uta'mo'ka'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ pata yau, mɨrɨpan ekota'ma'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, itɨ'pʉ patawon piya' tʉtʉrawasooi epose. Mɨrɨpan uya tikʉn non peiruku amʉ' ewe'se'na ennoko'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan nʉ'kwɨ esi'pʉ peiruku amʉ' i'kiyari pɨ' enta'napai. E'tane ɨnʉ' uya rɨ irepa'pʉ pen iti'kiyari ke.</li>
      <li>Isenuminkato' uya nin si eporo'pʉ mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan uya, ‘Ukʉipʉnʉ apiyo' ton i'kiyari esi serɨ eke pe rɨ to' entai rɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya. ‘E'tane si, serɨ yau apʉ'ka'nɨ pɨ' esi.</li>
      <li>Enna'po serɨ, tase'na ukʉipʉnʉ pɨ'; Papai, e'makoimasa' man Papa winɨkʉi' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨwinɨkʉi' nɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨmu tukai' uyesakʉi, e'tane pʉra ayapiyo' ton tonpa pe uku'kɨ.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ tʉkʉipʉnʉ piya'. “Ɨnnɨ rɨ marɨ iye'tane, ikʉipʉnʉ uya ensa' esi'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan tense isentu'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan eka'tumʉ'pʉ a'sise'na. Mɨrɨ tʉpo, ereutanʉkʉ'pʉ iya, a'su'kapɨtʉ'pʉ iya etupa pe.</li>
      <li>Imu uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', ‘Papai, e'makoimasa' man Papa winɨkʉi' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨwinɨkʉi' nɨrɨ. Ɨmu tukai' uyesakʉi.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan e'tane ikʉipʉnʉ uya ta'pʉ tapiyo' ton pɨ', ‘Inke pʉra wakʉ ipon ine'tɨ' ipontɨ kon pa, irimuui ɨntʉtɨ' itemiyatʉ pɨ'. Wakʉ ke kuru isapatooi'tɨtɨ'.</li>
      <li>Eka'nʉ'sa' paka ine'tɨ' iwɨnɨ kon pa. Enta'nanpai'nokon umu uye'sa' pɨ'!</li>
      <li>Pʉse rɨ si umʉre ima'tasa' kasa, iye'sa' rʉ'pʉ e'mʉ'sa'kasa' pe rɨ upona iyesi pɨ'. Itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ e'seposa',’ ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan kon e'sara'tɨ'pʉ enta'nan pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ koro'tau si, eke imu esi'pʉ mɨrɨ umɨ yau. Ɨutɨ piya' a'ko pe iye'sa' a'tai, wai uturumʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉumanunsan eta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya tapiyo' ton tonpa kɨ'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ekama'po'pʉ iya, ‘Ɨ'rɨ ne'ku'an?’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan eikʉ'pʉ iya, ‘Ayakon enna'posa'. Mɨrɨ pɨ' eka'nʉ'sa' paka wɨsa' ɨkʉipʉnʉ uya, atu' pe rɨ iyenna'posa' pɨ',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ewonpai pʉra irui usakorotasa' esi'pʉ. “‘Ewonkɨ,’ ka'se'na ikʉipʉnʉ epa'ka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan uya tʉkʉipʉnʉ eikʉ'pʉ, ‘Apʉne uyeta', amaimu pʉreme'nin pen sa'ne urɨ ko; ayapiyo' pe tʉuko'mansen inke rɨ wʉipiya ton kaisarɨ rɨ, e'tane utonpa ton pokon pe epori'mato' pe urepanin pen nɨ ɨmɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane si pʉse rɨ ɨmu ayapuruui, ɨpʉrataai ma'tanʉ'nin nʉ'pʉ ekuman pɨ', mɨrɨpan enna'posa' yo' pe, eka'nʉ'sa' paka mʉre wɨsa' auya,’ ta'pʉ iya. “Mɨrɨpan eikʉ'pʉ ikʉipʉnʉ uya,</li>
      <li>‘Upiyau te'sen ɨmɨrɨ tɨwɨrɨ rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon nɨ upiyau na'ne' mɨrɨ ɨiwano',’ ta'pʉ ikʉipʉnʉ uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>‘E'tane pʉse rɨ ayakon enna'posa' pɨ', itano'masa' rʉ'pʉ pe iyesi pɨ', ima'tasa' kasa rɨ iko'mansa' pɨ' epori'man,’ ta'pʉ ikʉipʉnʉ uya ipɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Panton ekama'pʉ Sises uya tʉpoitorʉ ton pana ya', se tawon: “Mɨrɨ yau ka'pon esi'pʉ ipʉrataaike', mɨrɨpan esi'pʉ timamin esa' ke. Tʉron nɨ a'tai, itepuru piya' ka'pon utɨ'pʉ tepuru pʉrataai mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itimamin ma'tanʉkʉ iya ekamai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ikɨ'ma'pʉ iya ekama'poto' pe tʉuya, ‘Ka'pon amʉ' uya upana'tɨsa' man ɨyeseru ke, mɨrɨpan apurɨsa' uya man. Ɨyenau iye'sa' rʉ'pʉ pʉrata mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uimamin apon nʉ'pʉ kareta ikonekaka'kɨ. Mɨrɨ enta' uimamin esa' pe ɨwe'to' oton pen mɨrɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan apiyo' usenuminka'pʉ, ‘Uyepuru uya, “Mɨrɨ enta' uimamin esa' pe ɨwe'to' oton pen mɨrɨ,” tasa' upɨ'. Ɨ'rɨ rɨ ku'to' pe uya ko? Pana' pe pʉra e'ai' sa'man tʉrawaso kupʉ uya poken pʉra, ɨpiyɨtʉ rɨ enkuui pe enasa' yau.</li>
      <li>Si'tuyai', uyepuru imamin anʉnnin nʉ'san pika'tɨ uya mɨrɨ, to' uya nɨrɨ upika'tɨto' pe, tiwʉ' kon ta' to' uya uyereutanʉ'to' pe rɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan uya te'mai' pʉra tepuru imamin e'ma'tɨnin nʉ'san kɨ'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uyee'pʉ tikin pa'ne. Wapiya iye'sa' ekama'po'pʉ iya, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ te'mai' pʉra uyepuru imamin arɨ'pʉ auya nai?’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>‘800 kiyaran e'to' airɨ are' kasi',’ ta'pʉ iya nin si mɨrɨ. “Mɨrɨpan pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, ‘Se si imenuka' 400 kaisaron iten karapa, are' kasi' tukai',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ tʉpo, ite'ma'pʉ pe iye'sa' ekama'po'pʉ iya, ‘Ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ te'mai' pʉra uyepuru imamin arɨ'pʉ auya nai?’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'. “‘1,000 kaisa rɨ pʉrowa paikii,’ ta'pʉ iya. “Mɨrɨpan pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, ‘Se si imenuka' 80 kaisa rɨ pʉrowa paikii tukai',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan etasa' itepuru uya a'tai, apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya, ɨri ku'sa' iya rɨ e'tane, tʉuko'manto' e'ma konekasa' iya pɨ'. Serɨ ta uya apʉne pʉra serɨ non pon kon esi emiya'poke' ton non eseru wenai uta'kwarʉkan pɨ' te'san, Papa munkɨ uta'kwarʉka non eseru pɨ' pʉra rɨ nin iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Ta uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨpʉrataai kon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨimamin kon ke entu'manin nan ipika'tɨtɨ' tʉtonpa ke ɨwesi kon pa, mɨrɨpan ɨpʉrataai kon u'ma'sa' a'tai, Papa uya ɨrepato' kon pe apata kon ke Epʉn po.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ aiko pe irepasa' uya wakʉ pe ikupʉ yau, eke ke irepa rɨ mɨrɨ wakʉ pe ikupʉ iya pɨ', e'tane ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉrɨ tʉrepasa' ma'tanʉ'nin nʉ'pʉ repa pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ eke ke.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa si serɨ non pon pʉrata mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mamin ma'tanʉ'nin pe ɨwesi yau, Papa uya wakʉ nin si ɨimamin ke Epʉn pon ke ɨrepa pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon imamin ma'tanʉ'sa' auya yau, ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨrepa ɨimamin ke kupʉ auya?</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ iyapiyo' pe te'sen esi pʉra iyesi asa'ron kon tepuru ton apiyo' pe. Tikin nan ewaruma'tɨ iya, isakon i'nʉnka iya; tikin nan pɨ' ita'si, isakon sanoma iya pʉra. Asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ Papa mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pʉrata apiyo' pe ɨwesi kon pʉra iyesi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ta Sises uya etasa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, Pari'si amʉ' uya isapema'pʉ, apʉne pʉra pʉrata i'nʉnkanin nan pe tesi kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon kuru sa'ne si kamoro ko wakʉ pe te'ku'san ka'pon amʉ' enu airɨ, e'tane Papa uya ɨi'tu kon pʉrata i'nʉnka auya'nokon ti'nʉnka auya'nokon entai, tukai'. Ka'pon uya wakʉ tato' ipɨ' pɨ', Papa uya ɨri ta.</li>
      <li>“Main Mosi' winon mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pu'kena' amʉ' Maimu esi'pʉ meruntɨ pe, Isaan Pa'tes uyepʉ pʉ'kʉ pona; mɨrɨ si'kɨrɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ekareei usekamasa' serɨ, mɨrɨpan pɨkɨrɨ e'pai tu'kan kon nɨ uta'kwarʉkan pɨ' man.</li>
      <li>Sa'man pe pʉra rɨ iyesi Epʉn mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non pʉra iyena aiko pe rɨ na'ne' pen nʉwarai'ka'pʉ uta'mo'ka pen Main apai.</li>
      <li>“Ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉno'pʉ nonkayai'ne' mɨrɨpan uya tʉron nɨ uri'san mari'ma, ekuma pe iyesi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon inonkasa' rʉ'pʉ mari'mayai'ne', ekuma pe iyesi,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ka'pon esi'pʉ moro imaminke', tʉtariren mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ rɨ ipon renen tato', epe'kena' ton nɨ. Eke pe rɨ iti'kiyari esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Moro kanan si entu'manin esi'pʉ mɨrɨ, ipon pʉn, itimamin pʉn, iti'kiyari pʉn, erekʉ'pan, Ʉrasaras itese'. Mɨrɨpan nin si tase to' uya inɨnpɨtʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ, imaminkena' mʉra'ta nau.</li>
      <li>Enta'napai iyesi'pʉ ipʉrataaikena' ka'pon i'kiyari punu'pɨ pɨ'. Pero amʉ' uye'pɨtʉ'pʉ iterekʉʉi ami'kai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ koro'tau, iyeri'kaa'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan nin si arɨ'pʉ inserʉ amʉ' uya, Papa apurɨnin nan eri'sa' utɨse' ya'. Mɨrɨ yau nin si, Ʉrasaras uya Epʉra'an tʉtɨpiya eporo'pʉ mɨrɨ pena ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ. Imaminkena' rɨ nɨrɨ eri'kaa'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ekepu u'na'tɨ'pʉ to' uya,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ apo' ya', ɨsɨ pata ya'. Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ si tenu tʉrʉ'pʉ iya mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan uya Epʉra'an piyau Ʉrasaras ene'pʉ ɨnnɨ kuru tʉpiyapai.</li>
      <li>‘Papai, Epʉra'an, upɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ! Ʉrasaras enno'kɨ tuna ka' temiyatʉ tʉki'se uyesen amankai' iye'to' pe. Ɨsɨ yau e'ai' a'ne' yau,’ ta'pʉ iya nin si mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“‘Mooi, mi'tuyan pe' nurɨne ɨwesi a'tai, pori' pe rɨ ɨuko'mamʉ'pʉ, Ʉrasaras kanan ɨri rɨ moronka pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan e'tane nin si, serɨ yau wakʉ pe rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ, ɨmɨrɨ kanan si ɨsɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pona ɨpiya' utɨn poken pʉra e'nɨ serɨ awonsi'kɨ, yaranta uya uwa'kʉ'sa' kon, uya'sanau'nokon iyesi. Ɨnʉ' rɨ utɨ poken pʉra miyarɨ. Mɨrɨ apai nɨrɨ serɨ ya' ɨnʉ' rɨ uyepʉ poken pʉra,’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ pɨ' ita'kwarʉka'pʉ ipan pe, ‘Warai yau ken si, Ʉrasaras enno'kɨ ukʉipʉnʉ iwʉ' ta'</li>
      <li>5 kaisaron kon uyakon non panamase'na, serɨ ya' to' uyepʉ namai'. Wakʉ pe to' uko'manto' pe, Papa Maimu awɨrɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan pɨ' Epʉra'an uya ta'pʉ, ‘Moro rɨ Mosi' maimu rʉ'pʉ esi mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pu'kena' amʉ' maimu rʉ'pʉ esi mɨrɨ, tɨwɨ to' netai, iyawɨrɨ te'to' kon pe,’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“‘Kane, Papai Epʉra'an, mɨrɨ apurɨ to' uya pʉra rɨ iyesi, serɨ awon kuru nin tɨ, ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ e'mʉ'sa'kasa' uya tauro'ka kon a'tai, to' uya kuru rɨ nin apurɨ mɨrɨ tʉmakooi kon apai rɨ nin si to' era'tɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya nin si mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan pɨ' Epʉra'an uya ta'pʉ, ‘Mosi' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pu'kena' amʉ' auro'ka'pʉ Papa uya, to' uya imenukato' pe, mɨrɨ awɨrɨ pʉra to' esi a'tai, uruwai' awon nɨ e'mʉ'sa'kasa' e'tane to' uya nɨrɨ imaimu etato' oton pen nɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya nin si mɨrɨ ipɨ',” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Makoi ya' ka'pon uta'mo'kato' rɨ e'ku'to' pe iyesi, e'tane nin si ɨsɨ yau kʉrɨ man tɨ iye'kupʉ emapu'tɨnin nʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Wakʉ iwa pe rɨ iyesi eno'ma a'tai parau ka' tɨ' a'nai' e'pato' yai tewa'tɨi' i'mʉ pɨ' pʉsamoro aiko ton nʉ'kwɨ tonpa e'makoima emapu'tɨ iya entai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, ti'tui' e'tɨ'. “Ɨtonpa e'makoimasa' a'tai, auro'kakɨ mɨrɨ enta' ikupʉ iya namai'; tʉmakooi apai iyera'tɨsa' a'tai, ipɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ.</li>
      <li>Tikin nan wʉi yau inke rɨ ɨpɨ' iye'makoimapɨtʉ a'tai, mɨrɨpan enna'popɨtʉ ɨpiya' a'tai, ‘Umakooi apai era'tɨsa' man,’ tase'na ipɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Itekare ekamanin nan pe enno'sa' kon uya ta'pʉ, “Ina Epuru, ina uya apurɨto' iku'kɨ eke pe,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Apurɨto' auya'nokon esi yau, aiko rʉ'kwɨ mosta' ena'pɨ kasa, ta auya'nokon nɨ mɨrɨ yʉi, morʉperi tato' ye' pɨ', ‘Ekuru'ka', parau ka' ɨye'pɨmɨ pa,’ ta auya a'tai, amaimu awɨrɨ rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>“Iya'tai pʉra, tʉpoitorʉ ke ɨtonpa e'sa' yau non anɨnin mɨrɨ pe pʉra karimeru amʉ' pa'simanin. Iyenna'posa' a'tai umɨ apai, ‘Ɨsi'kɨ ereutakɨ enta'nai',’ tawon pe' ɨmɨrɨ? Kane.</li>
      <li>Ta auya ipɨ', ‘Ui'kiyari ikoneka' unta'napa pa, mɨrɨ tʉpo rɨ nin si, ɨyenta'na parɨ,’ tawon ɨmɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Tenki tato' auya pʉra rɨ iyesi ɨpoitorʉ pɨ' amaimu awɨrɨ iye'sa' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon kanan mɨrɨ kasa rɨ ɨwe'to' oton kon mɨrɨ Papa uya ɨnkupʉnʉ kon ke ɨrepasa' kon i'ma'kasa' auya'nokon yau, ta auya'nokon nin si mɨrɨ, ‘Sepa' nan nʉ'kwɨ rɨ nin sa'ne ina, ina uya tʉtʉrawasooi kon i'ma'kasa' man,’ ta auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨ koro'tau Surusiran pona, Sameriya mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Kiyarari a'sanawɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>eke iwa pata eporo iya koro'tau, 10 kaisaron kon erekʉ'pa' nan uya eporo'pʉ. Ɨnnɨ Sises piyapai to' e'soto'ka'pʉ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Sises, ina epuru, ina pɨ' ɨsentu'ma'!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' ensa' iya a'tai, ta'pʉ iya, “Entantɨ', ɨsekamatantɨ' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan piya' ɨusepi'tɨsa' kon nɨ man tato' pe to' uya,” ta'pʉ iya. To' utɨ koro'tau, to' usepi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tikin nan nin si enna'po'pʉ Sises piya' tʉusepi'tɨsa' tense, ipan pe kuru rɨ Papa apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises pʉta piya' ita'mo'ka'pʉ tenki ta tʉuya ekamanin pe, pʉse rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ Sameriya pon pe.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ekama'po'pʉ, “10 kaisaron kon pen pe' ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nʉsepi'tɨi? Nai kamo ken si ɨtonpa ton?</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' Esuwerʉ amʉ' enna'po tane pʉra rɨ ɨmɨrɨ rɨken Esuwerʉ pen nɨ nin enna'posa' Papa apurɨpɨ'se'na?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya ipɨ', “E'mʉ'sa'ka', enta. Papa apurɨ auya uya rɨ ɨyepi'tɨsa' man,” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ a'tai kanan, Pari'si amʉ' uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ a'tai Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe uyepʉ?” tukai'. Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Enton pʉra rɨ iyesi mɨrɨ Papa ena a'tai esa' wannɨ pe,</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ, ‘Serɨ ne' ko,’ mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Mɨrɨ ne' ko,’ ta pʉra rɨ iyesi, apʉne pʉra, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe esi ɨyewan kon yau rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Iweyu uye'nɨ pɨ' man Ka'pon, Papa winon ɨnenpai ɨwe'to' oton kon, e'tane ento' auya'nokon oton pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' uya tato' oton, ‘Mɨ airɨ man,’ mɨrɨ pe pʉra, ‘Se airɨ man,’ e'tane ta to' uya pɨkɨrɨ rɨ kɨtɨpɨ'tʉu.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon weyu e'seposa' a'tai, kamiri' e'wei'tɨ uya ka' a'kwaka ipʉ'kʉ pona'ne kasa kuru iyesi mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane wapiya tanporon nɨ e'ne' moronkato' iya esi, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ serɨ a'taino kon uya ewaruma'tɨto' pe rɨ iyesi.</li>
      <li>“Nowa a'tai iyesi'pʉ na'ne' kasa kuru, mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ iye'to' oton Ka'pon, Papa winon weyu a'tai.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ uta're'tɨn pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ emari'man pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ e'tʉrʉn pɨ' emari'man nɨto' yau Nowa ewomʉ a' ya' weyu pona rɨ. Mɨrɨ a'tai, eke pe i'mʉnpʉ uyee'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya tanporo to' ma'tanʉkʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Iyepʉ rawɨrɨ Ra' a'tai iyesi'pʉ kasa rɨ marɨ iye'to' oton. Ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ uta're'tɨn pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kʉrʉpo'po pɨ', e'pɨn nɨ pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨutɨ amɨpɨtʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane Ra' uya Satan nɨmɨ'pʉ tʉpo, apo' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ sorʉ'pa uyee'pʉ Epʉn poi mɨrɨ to' ma'tanʉ'se'na.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ kasa kuru iye'to' oton Ka'pon, Papa winon usenpoika weyu a'tai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wʉi a'tai, ɨnʉ' rɨ tiwʉ' nakapu po na'ne' kʉu'tɨnin tiwʉ' tawon timamin kan. Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ kanan, ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉmainarʉ yau na'ne' nɨrɨ kʉsenna'ponin pata pona ɨ'rɨ kan nɨ.</li>
      <li>Ra' no'pʉ esi'pʉ na'ne' kuru nesii ɨyenu kon yau, timamin pɨ' iyera'tɨpɨ'sa' rʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉuko'manto' ɨnko'manʉ'paino uya inonkato' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉuko'manto' nonkanin uya ikoneka mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon: Mɨrɨ ewarupɨɨi tau, asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' e'to' oton te'nʉnto' kon apon po; tikin nɨ anʉnto' oton, isakon e'nɨnto' oton.</li>
      <li>Asa'ron kon uri'sami'si amʉ' e'to' oton a'nai' e'pa pɨ'; tikin nɨ anʉnto' oton, isakon e'nɨnto' oton.</li>
      <li>(Asa'ron kon kanan ka'pon amʉ' e'to' oton tʉmainarʉ kon yau. Tikin nɨ anʉnto' oton, isakon e'nɨnto' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.)</li>
      <li>“Nai airɨ, Itepuru?” ta'pʉ to' uya. To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Eke' airɨ rɨ anwana amʉ' amʉrato' oton,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises uya nin si panton ekama'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton enupanin pe tɨwɨrɨ rɨ tʉwɨpʉremasan pe to' e'to' pe tʉuseta'kai' pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Moro eseru aimenkanin esi'pʉ pata yau, Papa Maimu apurɨnin pen nɨ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' tʉusentu'masen pen nɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ esi'pʉ tɨwɨrɨ rɨ ata'kwarʉkai' tʉuye'pɨ'sen ipiya', ‘Upika'tɨkɨ uma'tanʉkʉ i'se na'ne' uyeyaton enapai,’ tapɨ'se'na.</li>
      <li>“Inke rɨ ipika'tɨ iya pʉra iyesi'pʉ, e'tane nin si isenuminka'pʉ mɨrɨ, ‘Apʉne pʉra tɨwɨrɨ rɨ itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ uye'pɨtʉ pɨ' uyewana'tɨse'na, mɨrɨ enta' nin si uyewana'tɨ iya pen mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ipika'tɨkapʉ uya serɨ i'se iye'to' ke, Papa namanin pe pʉra rɨ e'tane, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' tʉusentu'masen pe pʉra rɨ e'tane,’ ta'pʉ iya,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ' Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ɨsenupatɨ' ɨri, eseru aimenkanin pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ku'sa' iya pɨ' itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ pɨ', Papa nin si wakʉ eseru aimenkanin kamo ka'pon amʉ' tʉnanʉmʉ'san iwano' pe, tɨwɨrɨ rɨ tʉpika'tɨto' kon ekama'ponin nan. Tɨnɨn pɨ' iyesi pen nin kʉrɨ eseru aimenkanin kasa.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, Papa uya inke pʉra rɨ nin wakʉ kupʉ to' iwano' pe. E'tane, Ka'pon, Papa winon uyepʉ a'tai ken pe' si, ka'pon amʉ' rɨ pe' eporo iya tapurɨ pɨ', ɨpʉreman pɨ' serɨ non po?” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya panton ekama'pʉ wakʉ pe Papa enu yau tesi kon pe ekamanin nan pɨ', tʉron kon eno'mai'ma ɨri pe, se tawon,</li>
      <li>“Ɨpʉremai' asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' utɨ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' ta', tikin nan esi'pʉ Pari'si pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isakon esi'pʉ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin pe.</li>
      <li>Pari'si e'soto'ka'pʉ tʉpɨ' rɨ asauro'se tʉwɨpʉrema itese', ‘Papa, tenki ta uya serɨ ɨpɨ' tanporon kon entai rɨ wakʉ pe esi pɨ'. Tʉron kon man ɨri ton nɨ, makoi ku'nin nan nɨ, e'tane urɨ esi mentaino pe pʉra, kasi ye' pe pʉra, tekumasen pe pʉra, kʉrɨ rɨ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin kasa pʉra rɨ esi.</li>
      <li>Tʉuserumasen urɨ tenta'nai' pʉra asa'rɨ wʉi suntaaka a'sanau'ne, mɨrɨpan ɨrepato' tʉnin urɨ tasa' auya awɨrɨ uneporo'pʉ apai,’ tukai' iyɨpʉrema'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“E'tane pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin e'soto'kasa' esi'pʉ ɨnnɨ rɨ Pari'si piyapai, Epʉn winɨkʉi' tenu tʉrʉ'pʉ iya pen nɨ, e'tane tʉpʉropo wɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya tʉupokoita tʉmakooi ke tesi pɨ' ekamanin pe, ‘Papa, upɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ, urɨ sa'ne tʉmakooikenan,’ ta'pʉ iya.”</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, pʉse rɨ, isakon pen, ekonekasa' Papa pokon pe enna'po'pʉ, apʉne pʉra mɨ pe te'ku'sen ena mɨrɨ se pe rɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ se pe rɨ te'ku'sen ena mɨrɨ eke pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉmunkɨ kon nee'pʉ Sises uya to' a'pɨ'to' pe. Ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ ensa' a'tai, to' sanon ton eseremekʉ'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane rɨ, Sises uya mʉre amʉ' kɨ'ma'pʉ tʉpiya', “Tɨwɨ mʉre amʉ' nʉyepʉi upiya'; to' kʉsereutanʉ'tʉu, apʉne pʉra Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe kuru esi pʉsamoro waraino' nan iwano' pe.</li>
      <li>I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' rɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe eporo iya pʉra na'ne' mʉre kasa te'se, epa'kato' oton pen nɨ ya',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tikin nan itepuru uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ, “Wakʉ ti'sa, ɨ'rɨ kuru ku'to' uya esi wakʉ uko'man nɨto' tɨwɨrɨ rɨ, epoto' pe uya?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' wakʉ tukai' uyesakʉ auya?” tukai' Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ. “Ɨnʉ' pʉra rɨ iyesi wakʉ e'tane Papa rɨken.</li>
      <li>Mosi' nʉmenuka'pʉ i'tu auya: ‘Iyemari'masa' uri'san kʉsekumankai, ɨnʉ' rɨ kʉ'wɨnɨi, ama' pe kesii, kasi pe ka'pon pɨ' kasaurokʉi, ɨkʉipʉnʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asan nɨrɨ inamakɨ,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>“Mʉre' esi'pʉ si'kɨrɨ rɨ tanporo serɨ ton awɨrɨ rɨ uko'mansa' man,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' Sises uya a'tai, ta'pʉ iya ipɨ', “Tikin nan nɨken iyawɨrɨ ɨwe'to' e'ku'sa' man; tanporo ɨimamin pe na'ne' ikʉrʉpo'pomakɨ, mɨrɨpan itepe'pʉ tʉrʉ pa entu'manin nan ena', mɨrɨpan epe'pʉ pe wakʉ eporo pa Epʉn po. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' auya tʉpo, upɨkɨrɨ si ɨsi'kɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etasa' iya a'tai, ipan pe ika'nɨ' pʉra iyena'pʉ, apʉne pʉra imaminke' pe kuru iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Sa'man pe kuru rɨ iyesi imaminke' ton epa'ka poken pʉra Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya'!</li>
      <li>I'nai rɨ iyesi, sa'man pe pʉra rɨ kiyamerʉ epa'ka akusa enu euta awɨrɨ imaminke' epa'ka Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe ya' entai,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ etanin nʉ'san uya nin si ekama'po'pʉ mɨrɨ, “Ɨnʉ' kuru ken si epika'tɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Ka'pon pona sa'man pe na'ne' esi sa'man pe pʉra Papa pona,” ta'pʉ Sises uya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Tanporon nɨ sa'ne nɨnsa' ina uya ɨpɨkɨrɨ tʉutɨto' kon pe!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨnʉ' rɨ tʉpata'se' mɨrɨ pe pʉra tʉno'pʉ mɨrɨ pe pʉra takon non mɨrɨ pe pʉra tʉsanon mɨrɨ pe pʉra tʉmunkɨ ton nɨnnin nʉ'pʉ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe wenai,</li>
      <li>uya tu'ke ite'kwa rɨ serɨ a'tai teposen mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ serɨ enta' te'ton a'tai teposen tɨwɨrɨ uko'man nɨto' eporo pʉra iyesi ta pen nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya 12 kaisaron kon tʉpoitorʉ ton tʉpantakai' ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Utɨ'nokon serɨ Surusiran pona. Mɨrɨpan tanporon nɨ pu'kena' amʉ' nʉmenuka'pʉ Ka'pon, Papa winon pɨ' uta'ku'tɨto' oton mɨrɨ yau.</li>
      <li>To' uya itʉto' oton Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen ena', isapemato' oton to' uya, to' eta'tapɨ'to' oton ipona, to' uya ari'po'pɨ'to' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' uya rɨ iwɨto' oton.</li>
      <li>Itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai, iye'mʉ'sa'kato' oton kanan,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane ipoitorʉ ton uya serɨ to'ka'nʉkʉ pʉra rɨ iyesi'pʉ. Ɨ'rɨ kuru ta iya e'kwa pe mɨrɨ pɨ' isaurokʉ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Iseri'ko eporo koro'tau, tenku'nan esi'pʉ asanta ka'ta po eta'kwanʉn nɨ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' utɨ eta tʉuya a'tai, “Ɨ'rɨ ne'ku'an?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ', “Sises Nasare' pon utɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Sises, Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ, upɨ' ɨsentu'ma'!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises rawɨrɨ tʉutɨsan uya, “E'pana e'kɨ! Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' ɨukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ?” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'. Mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane ikɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Upɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ ta uya, Kin Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ!” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises e'takʉ'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya, “Kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon ine'tɨ' upiya',” ta'pʉ. Iye'sa' a'tai, Sises uya ekama'po'pʉ,</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ kupʉ uya i'se me'an ɨiwano' pe?” ta'pʉ iya. “Uyepuru, ennin pe e'pai e'ai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ', “Enkɨ si, Papa apurɨ auya uya rɨ ɨyepi'tɨsa' man,” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ta iya a'tai rɨ, ennin pe iyena'pʉ. Sises a'kɨrɨ itɨ'pʉ Papa apurɨpɨtʉi'ma. Kamo ka'pon amʉ' mɨrɨ ennin nʉ'san uya Papa kanan apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises si epa'kakaa'pʉ Iseri'ko pona, mɨrɨpan utɨ esi'pʉ iyawɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, ka'pon esi'pʉ, Sa'kiyas itese'. Kʉrɨ rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ pʉrata amʉranʉ'nin nan epuru pe, mɨrɨpan esi'pʉ ipʉrataaikena' pe.</li>
      <li>Sises ɨnenpai iyesi'pʉ, e'tane to'ken nʉ'kwɨ iyesi'pʉ tu'kan kon ka'pon amʉ' koro'tau. To'ken nʉ'kwɨ iyesi wenai, ene iya poken pʉra iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan nin si eka'tumʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ to' rawɨrɨ eke yʉi, si'kamorʉ itese' poi ekainʉnse'na mɨrɨ ponsi'kɨ ense'na. Mɨrɨ awɨrɨ rɨ Sises utɨ tukai' i'tu tʉuya ke.</li>
      <li>Sises uya mɨrɨ eposa' a'tai, tenu tʉrʉ'pʉ iya ka'takʉi', mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Sa'kiyas, inke pʉra ɨu'tɨkɨ. Serɨ pe ɨiwʉ' ta' utɨ serɨ aka'kʉranpai',” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan u'tɨ'pʉ imaimu awɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan uya pori' pe esii'ma tiwʉ' ta' ereutanʉkʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tanporo ka'pon amʉ' serɨ ennin nʉ'san etarerumʉ'pʉ, “Sises utɨsa' tʉmakooikenan iwʉ' ta' ika'kʉranpase'na,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya si tiwʉ' epoka'sa' a'tai, Sa'kiyas e'soto'ka'pʉ tase'na ipɨ', “Apʉne enkɨ, Uyepuru, serɨ awonsi'kɨ a'sa'mʉyai uimamin tʉku'se entu'manin nan repa uya mɨrɨ, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ rapumasa' uya pe iyesi yau, inna'po uya mɨrɨ asakɨrɨ'ne ite'kwa,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya nin si ta'pʉ mɨrɨ ipɨ', “Serɨ ɨutɨ tawon pika'tɨsa' Papa uya man serɨ pe, apʉne pʉra apurɨnin pe ɨwesi pɨ' Epʉra'an esi'pʉ kasa.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon, uye'sa' tʉmakooikenan kon warinpase'na mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ to' pika'tɨse'na,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉusaurokʉ etanin nʉ'san esi koro'tau, panton ekama pɨ' rɨ Sises esi'pʉ, a'ko pe Surusiran epokapʉ to' uya rɨ esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ka'pon amʉ' usenuminka'pʉ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe rɨ na'kɨ e'sara'tɨkapʉ serɨ pe rɨ ko tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ' panton ekama'pʉ iya se tawon: “Ka'pon eke ton mʉre pe iyentusa' rʉ'pʉ utɨ'pʉ ɨnnon nɨ pata ya' kin pe tanʉnto' pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tenna'poto' pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya 10 kaisa rɨ tʉpoitorʉ ton kɨ'ma'pʉ mɨrɨpan kon repa'pʉ iya 10 kaisa rɨ maina. ‘Serɨ pʉrata itʉrawasomatɨ' enna'po pʉ'kʉ pona,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane moro i'sero' kon pen esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya tʉtonpa kon amʉ' ennoko'pʉ ite'ma'pʉ tau. ‘Pʉse rɨ ka'pon i'se pʉra ina man kin, tepuru kon pe,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Kin pe iyenaka'sa' enna'po'pʉ tʉpata ya'. Mɨrɨpan uya tʉpoitorʉ ton tʉnrepa'san pʉrata ke kɨ'ma'pʉ, ɨ'rɨ kaisa rɨ to' uya ipiri'sa' tukai' ɨni'tupai iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Wapiyaro' uye'sa' uya, ‘Uyepuru, tikin nɨ urepa'pʉ auya ike piri'sa' uya man, 10 kaisa rɨ nin si maina esi,’ ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“‘Wakʉ kuru rɨ ku'sa' auya man, wakʉ upoitorʉ,’ ta'pʉ itepuru uya, ‘apʉne pʉra aiko rʉ'kwɨ ɨrepa'pʉ uya piri'sa' auya pɨ', 10 kaisaron pata esa' pe e'kɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Tʉron nɨ kanan ipoitorʉ uyee'pʉ tase'na ipɨ', ‘Uyepuru, tikin nɨ urepa'pʉ auya ike piri'sa' uya man, 5 kaisa rɨ ipona,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Itepuru uya ipɨ', ‘Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', 5 kaisaron pata esa' pe e'kɨ,’ ta'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Tʉron nɨ rʉ'pʉ kanan ipoitorʉ uye'kaa'pʉ tase'na ipɨ', ‘Uyepuru, serɨ si ɨiwano' maina; iko'manʉ'sa' uya tonanse, pon piya'pɨ po.</li>
      <li>Ɨpɨ' enari'nʉmʉ'pʉ, apʉne pʉra sa'man pe rɨ ɨwesi pɨ'. Anpata'tɨ'pʉ pen nɨ mo'kanin mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnpɨmɨ'pʉ pen nɨ anʉnnin,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan pɨ' itepuru uya ta'pʉ, ‘Amaimu ke rɨ ɨyeseru aimenka uya mɨrɨ, ɨmɨrɨ ɨri rɨ ipoitorʉ! I'tu auya si sa'man pe esi, unpata'tɨ'pʉ pen nɨ mo'kanin pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ unpɨmɨ'pʉ pen nɨ anʉnnin pe?</li>
      <li>Ɨ'rɨ pe ken iyesi pɨ' upʉrataai tʉtʉse tʉnonkai' pʉra ɨwesi'pʉ pʉrata epiri'to' iwʉ' ta', uye'sa' a'tai nin si iyepiri'sa' simo'kai'no?’ ta'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨpan uya nin si mɨrɨ yau iye'soto'kasa' kon pɨ' ta'pʉ, ‘Mɨrɨ itenau na'ne' maina imo'katɨ' itʉrʉ kon pa kʉrɨ 10 kaisaron maina esa' pe na'ne' ena',’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“‘Ina epuru, eke pe sa'ne epoka'sa' iya man ko,’ ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, ‘Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, tanporon kon itesa' pe te'san repa mɨrɨ miyarɨ rɨ ipona, e'tane kʉrɨ ɨ'rɨ esa' pen nɨ enapai imo'ka mɨrɨ itenawon nʉ'kwɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kamoro ui'se pʉra iye'sa' kon nʉ'san kin pe, uyeyaton non, kota'ma uya mɨrɨ. To' ine'tɨ', mɨrɨpan kon tʉ'ka kon pa uyenu airɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ panton ekama iya tʉpo, to' pokon pe Sises utɨ'pʉ Surusiran pona.</li>
      <li>Pe'pake mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Pe'tani eporo iya koro'tau i'kʉrʉ Are' Wʉpʉ tato' airɨ, asa'rɨ tʉpoitorʉ ton ennoko'pʉ iya, tai'ma to' pɨ',</li>
      <li>“Entantɨ' ɨyentau'nokon na'ne' eke iwa pata ya'. Mɨrɨ yau ɨyepa'ka kon pe rɨ isa'ka'si mʉre ewa'tɨsa' eporo auya'nokon mɨrɨ, ɨnʉ' rɨ utɨ'pʉ rʉ'pʉ pen ipo. Teukai' mʉne'tʉi' serɨ ya'.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' uya rɨ ɨyekama'po kon yau, ‘Ɨ'rɨto' pe euka auya'nokon?’ tukai', ‘Itepuru esi i'se,’ mʉkatʉi',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Kamoro si enno'sa' kon uya eporo'pʉ mɨrɨ tasa' iya rʉ'pʉ awɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>To' uya euka tane, itesanon uya to' ene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe euka auya'nokon?” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>“Itepuru esi i'se,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' uya ine'kaa'pʉ Sises piya', tʉpon kon tʉpɨtʉ'pʉ to' uya isa'ka'si a'poi pona, mɨrɨpan pona Sises tʉrʉ'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Itɨ koro'tau, ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉpon kon ta'nʉkʉ'pʉ asanta tawɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>A'ko pe si Are' Wʉpʉ piyapai, tʉutɨsen asanta epokapʉ iya a'tai, anpisin pe te'san ipoitorʉ ton e'sara'tɨ'pʉ Papa apurɨpɨtʉ pɨ', tʉukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨ'se eke pe, pori' pe tesi kon pɨ', apʉne pʉra tanporon nɨ eke Papa tʉrawasooi rɨ ku'pɨ'sa' Sises uya ensa' tʉuya'nokon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Pori' pe kin esi Itepuru ese' yau nʉye'ai'ne'!” “Tʉusewankamai' pʉra Epʉn yau nesii, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke pe iku'to' nesii ka'tau!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon si Pari'si amʉ' anpisin koro'tau te'san uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ti'sa, ɨpoitorʉ ton e'paka'to' pe to' esereme'kɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “To' e'paka'sa' a'tai, tɨ' amʉ' rɨ nɨrɨ e'sara'tɨ mɨrɨ ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨ' nɨ pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya si Surusiran enkapʉ esi'pʉ, Are' Wʉpʉ ponsi'kɨ, mɨrɨ pata awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' wenai ikaramʉ e'sara'tɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ,</li>
      <li>“Serɨ pe rɨ ito'ka'nʉ'sa' auya'nokon a'tai, ɨ'rɨ uya usewankaman pʉra na'ne' kupʉ tukai', Papa uya rɨ ɨusewankama kon pʉra rɨ ikupʉ, e'tane serɨ pe Papa uya ito'ka'nʉkʉ auya'nokon namai' onansa' man.</li>
      <li>Iweyu uye'nɨ pɨ' man ɨsɨ rɨ e'ku'to' oton ɨpɨ'nokon, ɨyeyaton kon amʉ' uya tɨ' amʉ' ka'to' oton apata'se' kon woi tekainʉnto' kon ipoi pe ɨwɨse'na'nokon. Sen winɨ'ne rɨ to' uya awa'kʉ'pɨ'to' oton kon ayainʉmʉ kon poken pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>To' uya ama'tanʉkʉ kon apata'se' kon pokon pe rɨ, ipʉra rɨ to' uya ima'tanʉ'to' oton enpɨ'ton pʉra rɨ, apʉne pʉra Papa uye'to' ɨpika'tɨi'nokon to'ka'nʉ'sa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ewomʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta', mɨrɨpan e'sara'tɨ'pʉ kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' te'san enpa'kapɨtʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Iye'menukasa', ‘Uiwʉ' e'to' esi ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pe,’ tawon; e'tane ‘ama' amʉ' en pe rɨ’ iku'sa' auya'nokon man!” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Wʉi kaisarɨ rɨ, enupan pɨ' iyesi'pʉ use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' tau. E'tane Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton, Main pɨ' enupanin nan, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' koro'tau te'san itepuru ton esi'pʉ ɨnwɨpai,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan e'tane ama'ai iwɨto' tʉuya'nokon eporo i'se to' e'tane, to' uya eporo pʉra iyesi'pʉ, apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' esi'pʉ ipan pe rɨ imaimu eta pɨ'.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Tʉron nɨ wʉi a'tai kanan, ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wakʉ itekare ekama pɨ' Sises esi koro'tau use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ tau. Papa ena' use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton, Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton uyee'pʉ ipiya',</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan kon uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ meruntɨrʉ winɨ serɨ ton kupʉ auya; ɨnʉ' uya serɨ meruntɨ ke ɨrepa'pʉ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Entakanoma'pʉ iya, “Ɨyekama'po uya 'nokon nɨ marɨ. Ekamatɨ' upɨ',</li>
      <li>Isaan uya pa'taisiman nɨto'—Epʉn winon pe pe' iyesi'pʉ, ka'pon winon pe katɨ iyesi'pʉ?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon usaurokʉ'pʉ tiwano' kon pe, “‘Epʉn winon’ ta pe iyesi yau, ekama'pon nɨ iya, ‘Ɨ'rɨ pe ken iyesi pɨ' apurɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi'pʉ?’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane, ‘Ka'pon amʉ' winɨ’ ta pe iyesi yau, ka'pon amʉ' uya nin si uwɨnɨ'nokon mɨrɨ tɨ' ke, apʉne pʉra Isaan apurɨ to' uya pu'kena' Papa winon tukai',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya nin si Sises maimu eikʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ, “Ewai' nawon, ina uya i'tu pʉra rɨ man nai winon pe iyesi'pʉ tukai',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ekamasa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi ke, ekama uya pʉra rɨ kanan iyesi ɨpɨ'nokon ɨ'rɨ meruntɨrʉ winɨ serɨ ton kupʉ uya tukai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' panton ekama'pʉ iya, “Ka'pon uya kʉre' itese' si'na' pe te'sen kiyari ye' patama'pʉ tʉmainarʉ yau, mɨrɨpan tʉrʉ'pʉ iya umɨ pɨ' te'san ena'. Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ tʉron nɨ pata ya' ɨko'manse'na inke rɨ.</li>
      <li>Iyakʉ'pʉsa' anʉmʉ weyu e'seposa' a'tai nin si, tʉpoitorʉ enno'kaa'pʉ iya umɨ tʉrʉ'pʉ tʉuya itena' ton piya' tʉrepato' pe to' uya tʉmainarʉ yawon ke, e'tane si kamoro uya ipanta'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ennoko'pʉ to' uya itemiyatʉ arʉ pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kanan tʉron nɨ tʉpoitorʉ enno'kaa'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan kanan panta'ma'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨri pe rɨ to' uya ikupʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan enna'po'pʉ itemiyatʉ arʉ pʉra rɨ marɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane, to' osorʉwano pe tʉron nɨ kanan tʉpoitorʉ enno'kaa'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan nɨ marɨ panta'makaa'pʉ to' uya ɨsɨ pe kuru rɨ, mɨrɨpan enpa'ka'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Mɨrɨ a'tai kiyari e'kwa esa' uya ta'pʉ, ‘Ɨ'rɨ ken si kupʉ uya serɨ? Uni'nʉnkanʉ rɨ nin si umu ennoko uya serɨ; to' uya nin si inama mɨrɨ,’ ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane si to' uya ensa' a'tai, ipɨ' to' usaurokʉ'pʉ. ‘Pʉse rɨ kuru pʉse rɨ inonka'pʉ anʉnton. Iwɨpai'nokon, inanʉmʉnʉ kiyari pata'se' anʉnto' kon pe uiwano' kon pe,’ ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan nin si eno'ma'pʉ to' uya kiyari e'kwa yapai, mɨrɨpan wɨnɨ'pʉ to' uya. “Ɨ'rɨ ken si kupʉ kiyari e'kwa esa' uya mɨrɨ to' pɨ':</li>
      <li>Iye'to' oton si, kamoro itesa' pe tʉnnonka'san tʉ'kase'na, mɨrɨpan uya tʉron kon ena' kiyari e'kwa nonkato' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya. Ka'pon amʉ' uya serɨ etasa' a'tai, “Serɨ e'pai pʉra rɨ man!” ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' ene'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Ɨ'rɨ ken si ta e'kwa pe iye'menukasa' esi: “‘Ɨutɨ amɨnin nan neno'ma'pʉ rʉ'pʉ tɨ' enasa' itekun airɨ te'sen tɨ' pe,’ tawon?</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon mɨrɨ tɨ' pona nʉta'mo'kayai'ne' nan utakiti'kwa mɨrɨ, e'tane ipona tɨ' nʉta'mo'kayai'ne' uta'si'kɨrɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Main pɨ' enupanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton esi'pʉ inke pʉra a'sito' tʉuya'nokon ipɨkɨrɨ warinpa pɨ', apʉne pʉra serɨ panton ekamasa' iya tʉpɨ'nokon ta iya e'kwa pe tukai', e'tane to' enari'nʉmʉ'pʉ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>A'ko pe ipa'sima pɨ' to' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya wakʉ ton pe itese' ka'pon amʉ' ennoko'pʉ ama'ai Sises maimu etase. Mɨrɨ wenai eparankato' pe tʉuya'nokon Roman amʉ' kopʉnaai ena' a'sito' pe iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya Sises ekama'po'pʉ, “Ti'sa, ina uya i'tu ausaurokʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ enupan auya ipokenan pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' menkanin pen ɨmɨrɨ, e'tane Papa eseru pɨ' enupan auya i'napairon awɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ipoken pe' iyesi Sisa ena' pʉrata tʉtʉsen e'ma ina uya a'tai, kane katɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Tenku'tɨpai to' esi poro tense to' pɨ' ta'pʉ iya,</li>
      <li>“Apʉne, pʉrata pun enpoikatɨ' uyena'. Ɨnʉ' nai, ɨnʉ' ese' nai ipɨ'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Sisa,” tukai'. Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Mɨrɨ wenai, itʉtɨ' ken si Sisa ena' itiwano' pe rɨ te'sen, Papa ena' kanan itiwano' pe rɨ nɨrɨ te'sen tʉrʉi'ma,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, annau isauro'to' winɨ to' uya isa'mato' pʉra rɨ iyesi'pʉ. Mɨrɨpan kon usewansiuka'pʉ ei'pɨtʉ iya pɨ', mɨrɨpan kon e'pakaa'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Satu'si amʉ' tonpa ton eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan pʉra iyesi tawon nan uyee'pʉ Sises piya' ekama'pose'na.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ti'sa, Mosi' uya imenukasa' uiwano' kon pe, ka'pon rui eri'sa' yau, tʉno'pʉ tʉnonkai' imunkɨ pʉra, iyakon nʉ'pʉ uya tʉrui no'pʉ rʉ'pʉ mari'mato' pe iyesi imu'tanʉ'to' pe tʉuya tʉrui iwano' pe.</li>
      <li>Moro si 7 kaisaron kon ɨsirunan esi'pʉ. Wapiyaro' emari'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan erikʉ'pʉ imʉre pʉra.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan akon nʉ'pʉ uya ino'pʉ rʉ'pʉ mari'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kanan erikʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' osorʉwano rʉ'pʉ uya kanan imari'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kanan erikʉ'pʉ. Mɨrɨ kasa tanporo 7 pan kon uya imari'mapɨtʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan 7 pe rɨ to' erikʉ'pʉ tʉmunkɨ ke pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon e'ma'pʉ pe, to' no'pʉ rʉ'pʉ rɨ marɨ eri'kaa'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan nɨsa' a'tai, ɨnʉ' kuru no'pʉ pe ken si iyesi, tanporo 7 kaisaron kon uya imari'masa' pɨ'?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' entakanoma'pʉ, “Serɨ a'taino kon emari'ma, mɨrɨpan kon e'tʉrʉ emari'man nɨto' yau.</li>
      <li>E'tane nin si tɨ, kamo emenna' pe uko'man nɨto' yau te'san, wakʉ tato' kon Papa uya ipɨ', terikʉ kon tʉpo iye'mʉ'sa'kasa' kon emari'ma pen nɨ nin, mɨrɨ pe pʉra to' e'tʉrʉ pen nɨ nin emari'man nɨto' yau,</li>
      <li>apʉne pʉra mɨrɨ enta' to' erikʉ pen, inserʉ amʉ' kasa rɨ nin si to' esi. Papa munkɨ pe to' esi, eri'nɨ tʉpo e'mʉ'sa'kan nɨsa' munkɨ pe to' esi pɨ'.</li>
      <li>E'tane yu' epo'tɨ ekareei yau, Mosi' uya rɨ enpoikasa' iyeri'sa' kon e'mʉ'sa'ka, apʉne pʉra Itepuru esakʉ iya, ‘Papa, Epʉra'an e'to' itese' pɨ', Aisi' e'to' itese' pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Seko' e'to' itese' pɨ' tukai',’ ta'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Papa, iyeri'sa' kon e'to' itese' pɨ' pen, e'tane nurɨnan kon, apʉne pʉra tanporo ipona nurɨne to' esi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tʉron kon Main pɨ' enupanin nan uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ti'sa, wakʉ pe kuru ei'sa' auya man,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨnʉ' rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ enta' ɨnekama'popɨ'pai pʉra.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ pe iyesi pɨ' to' uya Kʉrai esi Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ pe ta?</li>
      <li>Tepi' uya rɨ ekamasa' Eren apon yau: “‘Itepuru uya ta'pʉ uyepuru pɨ': “Ereutakɨ uyenwo'netʉ winɨ,</li>
      <li>ɨyeyaton non ku'tane uya a'ta apon pe,”’ tasa'.</li>
      <li>Tepi' uya esakʉ ‘uyepuru’ tukai'; nai kasa ken si Tepi' pa rʉ'pʉ pe iyesi?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ' tanporon kon uya rɨ eta tane,</li>
      <li>“Ti'tui' e'tɨ' Main pɨ' enupanin nan pɨ'. Ɨpininpaino kon kusan tʉpon kon yau mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ, ‘Miyarɨ,’ ta i'sero' kon tʉpɨ'nokon kʉrʉpo'po pɨ' e'nɨ pata'se' yau, eke ton apon po te'san Esuwerʉ amʉ' usenupato' iwʉ' tau mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉnamasan pata'se' yau kuru te'san enta'nan a'tai'ne.</li>
      <li>Itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' kon nʉ'san iwʉ' ma'tanʉkʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan kon ɨpʉrema kusan pe rɨ wakʉ ton tato' pe tʉpɨ'nokon. Ipan pe rɨ mɨrɨ waraino kon ekota'mato' oton,” ta'pʉ Sises uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Sises uya tenu tʉsa' koro'tau, ipʉrataaike' ton uya pʉrata tʉrʉ ene'pʉ iya Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉrataai yen ya'.</li>
      <li>Entu'manin nʉ'kwɨ kanan itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ uya asa'ron nʉ'kwɨ aiko ton pʉrata, ka'pa pun tʉrʉ ene'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon; pʉse rɨ entu'manin nʉ'kwɨ itaan'pʉ ima'tasa' rʉ'pʉ uya itʉsa' eke pe tanporon kon nʉtʉrʉ'pʉ entai rɨ.</li>
      <li>Tanporo pʉsamoro uya itʉsa' eke rɨ nin tʉpʉrataai kon tonpa; e'tane kʉrɨ rɨ tekota'mato' apai rʉ'kwɨ rɨ tanporo rɨ tʉpiyawon tʉrʉ'pʉ tʉuko'manto' ipɨ' rʉ'kwɨ rɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises poitorʉ tonpa ton usaurokʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pɨ' wakʉ pe rɨ isene pɨ' tɨ' ke itamɨsa', Papa ena' use'man nɨsa' rʉ'pʉ ike ton nɨ usene wakʉ pe. E'tane Sises uya ta'pʉ,</li>
      <li>“Serɨ yau menyatʉi'ne' pɨ' nin si ta uya, iweyu e'seporo mɨrɨ mɨ pe rɨ tikin nɨ tɨ' e'nonkato' oton pen nɨ ɨsipʉro'po, tanporon nɨ uta'po'to' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, to' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Ti'sa, ɨ'rɨ a'tai serɨ ton e'ku'to' oton? Ɨ'rɨ kuru ken si esi ento' ipɨ' pe e'ku'ka'nɨ pɨ' iyesi ekamanin pe?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya: “Tenu ke e'tɨ' ɨyenku'tɨ kon namai'. Apʉne pʉra tu'kan kon nɨ uye'to' oton uyese' yau, ‘Urɨ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ,’ ka'se'na, mɨrɨpan, ‘Iweyu man a'ko pe,’ ta to' uya. To' pɨkɨrɨ ke'tʉu.</li>
      <li>Usewa'noman mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tepuru kon ɨneno'mapaino kon eta auya'nokon a'tai, kenari'nʉntʉu. Serɨ ton nɨ e'kupʉ mɨrɨ wapiya, e'tane inke pʉra pata weyu u'matʉ uyepʉ pen nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Tʉpataron kon uya tʉpataron kon nɨ nɨrɨ ewa'nomato' oton, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ esa' wannɨ pe te'san uya esa' wannɨ pe te'san nɨ nɨrɨ ewa'nomato' oton.</li>
      <li>Eke pe kuru rɨ tʉrʉ'pʉnʉ amʉ' iwankan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ paran amʉ' e'to' oton pata ton yau'ne' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ nari'panin nɨ e'ku'to' oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke rɨ ento' ipɨ' ton Epʉn apai e'to' oton.</li>
      <li>“E'tane serɨ rawɨrɨ, to' uya aya'sito' oton kon, ɨkota'mato' oton kon to' uya. Usenupan nɨto' iwʉ' ta' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ pariki'si ta', kin amʉ', kopʉna amʉ' rakʉi' nɨrɨ to' uya ɨtʉto' oton kon, tanporo serɨ esi uyese' uriya'.</li>
      <li>Uyekareei ekamato' auya'nokon oton to' pɨ' serɨ moron nʉ'pʉ pe.</li>
      <li>E'tane ekonekatɨ' rɨken pena rɨ ɨusewankama kon namai', nai kasa kuru si e'wapu'tɨ ta auya'nokon namai'.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra amaimu'tɨto' uya 'nokon oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyemeporʉ'tɨ uya 'nokon ausauro'to' kon ike ke ɨyeyaton kon uya, ‘Kasi pe ɨwesi,’ ta namai' ɨpɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon nɨ eparankato' oton asanon kon uya rɨ, ɨtonpa kon amʉ' uya rɨ. To' uya ɨtonpa kon tʉto' oton eri'nɨto' ya'.</li>
      <li>Tanporon kon ka'pon amʉ' uya rɨ ɨyewaruma'tɨto' oton kon urɨ uriya'.</li>
      <li>To' uya rɨ ɨwɨsa' kon e'tane, aya'kwarʉ kon nɨ mainanpa uya.</li>
      <li>Pana' pe ɨye'mʉ'sa'ka kon winɨ ɨuko'manto' kon eporo auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Soisa amʉ' amʉrasa' ene auya'nokon a'tai Surusiran woi, i'tu auya'nokon mɨrɨ to' uya ima'tanʉkʉ tukai'.</li>
      <li>Tɨwɨ kamoro Isutiya po na'ne' nan nainʉmʉi wʉ' ton pona'ne; tɨwɨ kamoro eke pata yawon kon nepa'kai, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kamoro pata yau na'ne' nan kʉsepa'kanin eke pata pona.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ta uya, apʉne pʉra mɨrɨ si e'to' oton, Papa uya Surusiran yawon kon kota'ma weyu pe, serɨ e'kupʉ mɨrɨ pu'kena' amʉ' nʉmenuka'pʉ a'ku'tɨ pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai'ne ɨsɨ pe kuru rɨ uri'sami'si amʉ' mono' pe te'san pona iye'to' oton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ mana' pokon kon imunkɨ pona. Ipan pe rɨ usewankaman e'to' oton non po, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ekota'man nɨto' e'to' oton pʉsamoro ka'pon amʉ' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Soisa amʉ' uya tu'kan kon nɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' tʉ'kato' oton, mɨrɨpan tʉron kon a'sisa' kon Esuwerʉ amʉ' ato' oton to' uya pata amʉ' kaisarɨ rɨ. Ka'pon amʉ', Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen uya Surusiran ma'tanʉ'to' oton ipan pe rɨ. To' uya ikupʉ weyu pe Papa nʉkupʉ'pʉ u'matʉ pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“I'tuto' ipɨ' ton e'ku'to' oton wʉi enu yau, kapʉi yau mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ sirikɨ amʉ' yau. Non po tʉpataron kon e'to' oton ɨsɨ rɨ i'tu pɨ', etʉipɨ' nɨ pɨ' parau a'merumʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iyenu'pɨtʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' enato' oton ɨ'sɨ'mʉra tetʉipɨtʉ kon ke, tʉuye'sen non pona i'tu tʉuya'nokon pɨ', apʉne pʉra ka' yawon kon nɨ usi'ki'mato' oton pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, to' uya Ka'pon, Papa winon ento' oton uyepʉ kapuru' yau tʉmeruntɨrʉ ke, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ eke rɨ a'kwarʉ pokon pe.</li>
      <li>Serɨ e'kupʉ e'sara'tɨ ene ɨmɨrɨ'nokon upoitorʉ ton uya a'tai, mepori'matʉi' si, itenupɨkɨrɨ esii'ma, apʉne pʉra serɨ esi a'ko pe rɨ Papa uya ɨpika'tɨto' kon esi ekamanin pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ' panton ekama'pʉ iya, “Apʉne kiyari ye' ito'ka'nʉ'tɨ'; tanporon nɨ sa'ne yʉi amʉ'.</li>
      <li>Itare'kasa' rʉ'pʉ atu'ta a'tai, tanporon kon uya i'tu iyepetato' oton tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ si tɨ, serɨ ɨsɨ ton e'kupʉ ene auya'nokon a'tai, i'tu auya'nokon kuru rɨ a'ko pe rɨ Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe weyu e'seporo.</li>
      <li>“I'napairon ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, serɨ a'taino kon kuru rɨ pʉra iyenato' oton pen nɨ serɨ ton e'kupʉ pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ.</li>
      <li>Tanporon nɨ ka' po na'ne', non po na'ne', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ non nɨ nɨrɨ pʉra iyenato' oton, e'tane umaimu mɨrɨ tereutaton pen nɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Ti'tui' e'tɨ', wakʉ pɨ' ɨusenuminkato' kon piyapai ayano'manin kon pɨ'. Ke'taripatʉu, e'tari ton nʉkupʉnʉ kʉ'ku'tʉu, serɨ non pon pɨ' rɨ aya'kwarʉ kon kʉsainʉnpatʉu. Mɨrɨ ku'sa' auya'nokon yau, iyekonekasa' pe pʉra rɨ ɨwesi kon koro'tau ɨyeporo uya 'nokon mɨrɨ ite'kwanau pʉra rɨ.</li>
      <li>Ɨpɨ'nokon iye'kupʉ pe pʉra kʉsekamatʉu, apʉne pʉra tanporon kon, mɨ yawɨron kon pɨ' rɨ iye'ku'to' oton mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wenai, ti'tui' rɨ tenu ke rɨ e'tɨ', ɨpʉrematɨ' Papa uya ɨpika'tɨto' kon pe ɨsɨ ton te'ku'sen awɨrɨ wakʉ pe ɨyepa'ka kon pa. Ɨpʉrematɨ' rɨ kanan wakʉ pe te'mʉ'sa'kasen pe ɨwesi kon pa Ka'pon, Papa winon rau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Wʉi kaisarɨ rɨ, ka'pon amʉ' enupa pɨ' Sises esi'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ tau. Ko'mamʉ pe'ne nin si tɨ, itɨpɨtʉ'pʉ Are' Wʉpʉ pona e'nʉnse'na.</li>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru rɨ kanan, tanporon kon tenupa iya 'nokon etanin nʉ'san uye'pɨtʉ'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ ta' tenupato' kon iya etase'na.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>A'ko pe si A'sarutanʉ'sa' Pen Pʉreti Pɨ' Enta'nan Weyu, To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ tato' pɨ' enta'nan weyu e'seporo esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan esi'pʉ Sises ma'tanʉ'to' tʉuya'nokon winɨ eporo i'se, ama'ai, apʉne pʉra ka'pon amʉ' pɨ' tenari'nʉmʉ kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, Se'tan ewomʉ'pʉ Isutas, Eskariya' tato' ipɨ' ya', 12 kaisaron kon ipoitorʉ ton tonpa pe te'sen.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Isutas utɨ'pʉ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pa'simanin nan piya'. Mɨrɨpan kon a'kɨrɨ usauro'nɨ pɨ' iyesi'pʉ Sises eparankato' tʉuya pɨ' to' uya a'sito' pe.</li>
      <li>To' epori'ma'pʉ, mɨrɨpan pʉrata ke irepa pɨ' to' e'kama'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya, “Ewai',” ta'pʉ, mɨrɨpan esi'pʉ Sises tʉto' tʉuya weyu eporo i'se, anpisin pe ka'pon amʉ' esi a'tai pʉra.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai A'sarutanʉ'sa' Pen Pʉreti Pɨ' Enta'nan Weyu e'seporo'pʉ karimeru mʉre wɨto' Itepoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ iwano' pe.</li>
      <li>Sises uya Pi'ta mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isaan ennoko'pʉ, tai'ma to' pɨ', “Entantɨ' enta'nan nɨto' To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ pɨ' ikonekatantɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>“Nai yau ken si ina uya ikoneka i'se ɨwesi ite'ma ta'?” tukai' to' uya ekama'po'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Eke pata pona ɨyepa'kasa' kon a'tai, ka'pon tuna yen anin uya ɨyeporo kon mɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan pɨkɨrɨ ɨutɨ newonyai'ne' ta' mʉtɨtʉi'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ɨutɨ esa' pɨ' mɨkatʉi', ‘Ti'sa man, nai yau tʉpoitorʉ ton pokon pe To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ pɨ' tenta'na kon tukai' ɨni'tupai.’</li>
      <li>Kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon uya ka'tawon eke ɨutɨ ekama mɨrɨ tanporon nɨ e'to' itau. Mɨrɨ yau si tanporon nɨ mʉkonekatʉi',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ nin si mɨrɨ, to' uya eporo'pʉ Sises uya ekama'pʉ poro rɨ. Mɨrɨpan kon uya si To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ pɨ' te'to' kon koneka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Iweyu e'sepoka'sa' a'tai, Sises mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoitorʉ ton enapɨtʉ'pʉ tʉteire' kon po tepʉrʉ piyau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Aya'kɨrɨ'nokon kuru rɨ enta'napai e'sa' serɨ To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ i'kiyari pɨ', ukota'ma to' uya rawɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, enta'nato' oton pen ipɨ' kanan, Papa na'ne' esa' wannɨ pe yau e'seposa' a'tai rɨken kanan enta'nan,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ko', waain yen anʉmʉ'pʉ temiyatʉ ya', mɨrɨpan uya tenki ta'pʉ Papa pɨ', mɨrɨpan tʉpo tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ' ta'pʉ, “Akaisarɨ'ne'nokon se waain, ko' yawon ensitɨ'.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra ekama uya ɨpɨ'nokon, iteperu euku ensito' uya oton pen, Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe uyepʉ pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya pʉreti anʉmʉ'pʉ, tenki ta'pʉ iya Papa pɨ', mɨrɨpan i'kwɨ'pɨtʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan ekamʉ'pʉ iya to' ena', tai'ma to' pɨ', “Serɨ serɨ upun iye'tʉsa' ɨiwano' kon pe; serɨ iku'tɨ' ɨyenu kon yau ukupʉ auya'nokon ekamanin pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ marɨ tenta'na tʉpo, ko' anʉmʉ'pʉ iya. To' pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Serɨ ko' esi emenna' pe ekonekan nɨto' umʉnʉ yau, ɨiwano' kon pe iye'kwansa'.</li>
      <li>E'tane kʉrɨ rɨ uyeparanka ton emiya esi uyemiya pokon pe rɨ tepʉrʉ po.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon, Papa winon utɨto' oton tʉpɨ' isekamasa' na'ne' kasa rɨ, e'tane ɨsɨ yau rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ ka'pon esi eparankanin,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ipoitorʉ ton usekama'popɨtʉ'pʉ, “Ɨnʉ' kuru rɨ si u'koro'tawon kon uya serɨ ku'to' oton?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon si e'sara'tɨ'pʉ tiwano' kon pe rɨ e'sei'pɨ' nɨ pɨ' ɨnʉ' kuru e'to' oton eke pe tukai'.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Kin amʉ' Esuwerʉ amʉ' pen esanon esi to' esa' pe, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ kamo tʉmeruntɨrʉ kon apurɨnin nan to' pɨ' e'sesakʉ ‘ka'pon amʉ' pika'tɨnin nan’ tukai'.</li>
      <li>E'tane mɨrɨ kasa ɨwe'to' kon pe pʉra iyesi. E'tane ru'ku, eke pe na'ne' ɨ'koro'tau'nokon e'to' pe iyesi a'mi'pɨ wannɨ kasa, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ esa' wannɨ, apiyo' wannɨ kasa.</li>
      <li>Ɨnʉ' rupɨ esi eke pe, iyereutasa' na'ne' enta'nan pɨ', mɨrɨ pe pʉra apiyo' wannɨ katɨ? Enta'nan pɨ' iyereutasa' na'ne' esi eke pe ɨpona, tʉusekansen entai, e'tane urɨ esi ɨpiyau'nokon tʉusekansen kasa.</li>
      <li>“Ɨmɨrɨ'nokon kamoro uya'kɨrɨ iye'sa' kon ui'tupɨ'to' yau'ne rɨ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan uya rɨ ɨkupʉ kon kin pe ɨwesi kon pa ukʉipʉnʉ uya rɨ uku'sa' na'ne' kasa itesa' pe e'to' pe,</li>
