      <li>ɨyenta'na kon pa mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ensi kon pa utepʉrʉʉi po esa' wannɨ pe e'to' yau mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨyereuta kon pa apono' po 12 kaisaron kon Esuwerʉ pon kon eseru aimenka pɨ',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Sises uya Pi'ta pɨ', “Saiman, Saiman,” ta'pʉ, “apʉne uyetakɨ. Se'tan uya Papa ekama'posa' man ɨi'tupɨ'to' kon pe tʉuya, ka'pon uya ta'nasi eisika kasa,</li>
      <li>e'tane ɨpʉremasa' man ɨpona, Saiman, anapurɨnʉ apai ɨyemo'ka namai'. Ɨyenna'posa' pe iyesi a'tai, ɨtonpa ton mʉmeruntɨtanʉkʉi' to' tauro'kai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Pi'ta uya ta'pʉ, “Uyepuru, e'kamasa' rɨ serɨ aya'kɨrɨ rɨ pariki'si ta' utɨto' pe mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uma'tato' pe rɨ aya'kɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ekama uya serɨ ɨpɨ', Pi'ta, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ rawɨrɨ serɨ pe, osorʉwau ite'kwa ui'tunin pe pʉra ɨye'ku'to' oton,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya to' ekama'po'pʉ, “Ɨyenno'sa' uya 'nokon a'tai, itekare ekamai', ɨpʉrataai kon pʉra, apaikii kon pʉra mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ asapatooi kon pʉra, ɨ'rɨ rɨ na'kɨ i'se ɨwe'to' kon mʉwarinpata'tʉi'nokon?” ta'pʉ iya. “Kane,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' nin si ta'pʉ iya, “Serɨ pe nin si tʉpʉrataai ke ɨwesi kon a'tai, atɨ' rɨ si aya'kɨrɨ'nokon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ apaikii kon nɨ kanan. Ɨsuparaai kon pʉra iyesi yau, ɨpon kon tʉkʉrʉpo'pomai' ɨsuparaai kon me'matʉi'.</li>
      <li>Ekama uya, iye'menukasa' na'ne' upɨ' uta'ku'tɨto' pe rɨ iyesi, ‘Ka'pon amʉ' uya ɨri ton main awɨron kon pen tonpa pe iyesi'pʉ tato' oton,’ tawon. Serɨ iye'menukasa' rʉ'pʉ urɨ pɨ' rɨ uta'ku'tɨ mɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Apʉne enkɨ, asa'rɨ rɨ supara man ina piyau,” ta'pʉ to' uya. “Mɨrɨ kasa rɨ si e'paka'tɨ', tʉron nɨ enna pɨ' kasauro'tʉu,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises utɨ'pʉ Are' Wʉpʉ airɨ'ne te'pɨ'to' kasa rɨ ipoitorʉ ton uya e'ma'pʉka'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Pata eposa' tʉuya'nokon a'tai, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Ɨpʉrematɨ', i'tupɨ'nɨto' ya' auta'mo'ka kon namai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tɨ' eno'mato' enta' rɨ itɨ'pʉ, iye'sekunka'pʉ ɨpʉremase'na.</li>
      <li>“Papai, ɨnku'pai ɨwesi yau, serɨ ko' imo'kakɨ uyenapai, e'tane i'se ɨwe'to' awɨrɨ iku'kɨ, i'se e'to' awɨrɨ pen,” ta'pʉ iya. [</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ta iya koro'tau, Papa inserʉʉi uyee'pʉ ipiya' imeruntɨrʉ'tɨi'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan Sises ɨpʉrema'pʉ ipan pe, tʉuta'kwarʉkai', apʉne pʉra pokoi pe tesi pɨ', mɨrɨpan eramu'ta usee'kwa esi'pʉ non pona mʉn kasa.]</li>
      <li>Tʉwɨpʉrema tʉpo, iye'mʉ'sa'kasa' utɨ'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton piya'. To' e'nʉnpɨ'sa' eporo'pʉ iya, pokoi uya to' eketu'kasa'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨto' pe ɨye'nʉmʉ kon? Te'mʉ'sa'kai' ɨpʉrematɨ', i'tupɨ'nɨto' ya' auta'mo'ka kon namai',” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Usauro'nɨ pɨ' rɨ marɨ iyesi koro'tau, anpisin uyee'pʉ to' piya', ka'pon, Isutas tukai' tesa'sen, 12 kaisaron kon tonpa pe te'sen esi'pʉ to' esa' pe. Sises piya' a'ko pe iyee'pʉ a'su'kase.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Isutas, Ka'pon, Papa winon pe' eparanka auya mɨrɨ uta'su'kan ke?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton uya te'ku'sen ensa' a'tai, Sises pɨ' ta'pʉ to' uya, “Ina epuru, ina uya pe' si to' panta'ma serɨ tʉsuparaai kon amʉ' ke?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' tonpa uya use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru poitorʉ pana enwo'ne' winon a'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises uya ta'pʉ tʉpoitorʉ ton pɨ', “Tɨwɨ nesii!” ta'pʉ iya. Mɨrɨpan uya a'pɨtʉ ke rɨ ipana epi'tɨ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru pɨ', use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pa'simanin nan mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ itepuru ton tʉkan iye'sa' kon pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Main awɨron kon pen pe' esa' pe esi serɨ, ɨuye'sa' kon na'ne' supara amʉ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ wa'tana amʉ' esa' pe?</li>
      <li>Wʉi kaisarɨ rɨ ɨpiyau'nokon esi'pʉ Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ tau. Upɨ' ɨyemiyatʉ kon tʉsa' auya'nokon pʉra iyesi. E'tane serɨ pe ɨweyu kon pe iyesi—ewarupɨ esi pana' pe ɨyesa' kon pe koro'tau,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'sise to' uya arɨ'pʉ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru iwʉ' ta'. Pi'ta uya e'ma'pʉka'pʉ ɨnnonsi'kɨ rɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane apo' po'tɨsa' to' uya a'tai pʉroroi aporo' po, mɨrɨpan kon ereutasa' esi'pʉ a'samʉtʉ yau, Pi'ta ereuta'pʉ to' piyau.</li>
      <li>To' poitorʉ uri'san uya iyereutasa' ene'pʉ apo' weyu ya'. Enpɨtʉ'pʉ iya a'ko pe esii'ma, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ, “Pʉse rɨ ka'pon ne'tai Sises a'kɨrɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane i'tunin pe pʉra iye'kuu'pʉ. “Ma'non, kʉrɨ rɨ i'tunin pen urɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Emennʉ'pʉ iwa rɨ, tʉron nɨ uya kanan ensa' esi'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ ipɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ sa'ne kʉrɨ rɨ ko to' tonpa,” ta'pʉ iya. “Mooi, kʉrɨ rɨ pen nɨ urɨ!” ta'pʉ Pi'ta uya.</li>
      <li>Tikin ite'kwa kʉra' emiya era'tɨ'pʉ tʉpo'ne rɨ, tʉron nɨ ka'pon uya e'se'ne' pe ipɨ', “I'napai rɨ sa'ne pʉse rɨ esi'pʉ iya'kɨrɨ; apʉne pʉra Kiyarari pon pe iyesi,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Pi'ta uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Mooi, ipɨ' masauro'atʉi'ne' i'tu uya pʉra rɨ man!” ta'pʉ iya. Usauro'nɨ pɨ' iyesi koro'tau, kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Itepuru era'tɨ'pʉ to'sa rɨ Pi'ta ense'na. Mɨrɨ a'tai si, Pi'ta uya Itepuru uya tauro'ka'pʉ rʉ'pʉ nee'pʉ tenu ya', “Kɨrɨtɨkɨ uturumʉ rawɨrɨ serɨ pe, osorʉwau ite'kwa unonkato' auya oton,” tawon.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan epa'ka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan ukaramʉ'pʉ ipan pe.</li>
      <li>Sises erasu pe te'san e'sara'tɨ'pʉ isapema pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ iwɨpɨtʉ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' uya itenu auromʉ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Pu'kena' pe ekamakɨ! Ɨnʉ' ɨwɨnɨi?” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon usaurokʉ'pʉ eke pe rɨ ɨri pe rɨ tʉsapemai'.</li>
      <li>Pata ema'sa' a'tai, ka'pon amʉ' epuru ton—asa'rɨ rɨ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan amʉra'pʉ, mɨrɨpan kon rakʉi' Sises arɨ'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>“Ina pɨ' ɨsekamakɨ, Kʉrai pe ɨwesi yau,” ta'pʉ to' uya. Sises uya to' eikʉ'pʉ, “Usekamasa' yau, uyapurɨ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi;</li>
      <li>ɨyekama'posa' uya 'nokon yau, uyeikʉ auya'nokon pʉra iyesi.</li>
      <li>E'tane serɨ awonsi'kɨ Ka'pon, Papa winon ereutato' oton meruntɨ pe te'sen Papa enwo'netʉ winɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Tanporo esii'ma to' uya ekama'po'pʉ, “Papa Mumu pe ken pe' si ɨwesi?” ta'pʉ to' uya. To' eikʉ'pʉ iya, “Ipoken me'atʉi' kʉrɨ rɨ pe esi mʉkayatʉi'ne',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, ta'pʉ to' uya, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe miyarɨ ekamanin i'se e'nɨ? Etaka'sa' sa'ne mɨrɨ ko inta apai,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kamoro si asauro'se iyamʉrasa' kon nʉ'san uya Sises arɨ'pʉ Paire' Isutiya kopʉnaai piya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ yau, eseru'tɨ pɨ' to' esi'pʉ, “Pʉse rɨ uya ka'pon amʉ' ano'ma, ‘Pʉrata kʉ'nonkatʉu pata esa' ena', urɨ kʉrɨ rɨ Kʉrai pata esa',’ ta iya,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Sises ekama'po'pʉ Paire' uya, “Esuwerʉ amʉ' kin pe' ɨmɨrɨ?” tukai'. Mɨrɨpan eikʉ'pʉ Sises uya, “Ewai', mʉkayai'ne' kasa rɨ,” tukai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Paire' uya ta'pʉ use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' pɨ', “Ɨ'rɨ rɨ pʉse rɨ wɨto' ipɨkɨrɨ eposa' uya pʉra man,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane Sises pɨ' rɨ usauro'nɨ pɨ' to' esi'pʉ, “Eke pe rɨ usewa'noman emapu'tɨ iya pata Isutiya poro rɨ to' enupa ke. Pata Kiyarari po iye'sara'tɨ'pʉ, mɨrɨpan uye'ka'sa' serɨ ya', mɨrɨ pɨ' rɨ to' enupa pɨ' iyesi,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>To' ekama'po'pʉ iya, “Sises pe' esi Kiyarari ko' pe?” tukai',</li>
      <li>“Ewai',” tasa' to' uya pɨ'. Sises ennoko'pʉ iya kin Era' piya', apʉne pʉra itesa' pe iye'to' winon pe iyesi pɨ', mɨrɨ koro'tau si Surusiran po Era' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan epori'ma'pʉ ipan pe Sises tense, apʉne pʉra inke rɨ Sises ɨnenpai te'sen pe iye'pɨtʉ'pʉ, apʉne pʉra eke Papa tʉrawasooi kupʉ iya tawon etasa' tʉuya pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan nin si kupʉ iya ɨnenpai iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan pɨ' rɨ Sises ekama'popɨtʉ'pʉ iya, e'tane eikʉ'pʉ iya pen.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Main pɨ' enupanin nan e'soto'pɨ'sa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ yau Sises eseru'tɨ pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Era' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ isoisaai amʉ' uya Sises sapema'pʉ. E'neimapɨtʉ pe to' usennaka'pʉ ipɨ', mɨrɨpan pontɨ'pʉ to' uya epe'kena' kuru pon ya', mɨrɨpan na'po'pʉ to' uya Paire' piya'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ wapiya Era' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Paire' pokon esi'pʉ ɨ'seyaton pe, mɨrɨpan kon ena'pʉ ɨsitonpa pe mɨrɨ wʉi a'tai rɨ.</li>
      <li>Paire' uya use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru, ka'pon amʉ' epuru ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon amʉ' rɨ nɨrɨ amʉranʉkʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' uye'sa' a'tai, ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ', “Pʉse rɨ ka'pon ne'sa' auya'nokon upiya', kopʉna ewa'nomanin pe ka'pon amʉ' kupʉ iya ta auya'nokon. Ekama'popɨ'sa' uya man apana airɨ'nokon, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨ'rɨ rɨ eposa' uya pʉra man meseru'tɨyatʉi'ne' ipɨ', pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Era' uya rɨ nɨrɨ ɨri pe man tasa' pʉra man, apʉne pʉra inna'posa' iya man upiya'nokon. Menyatʉi'ne' rɨ, ɨ'rɨ rɨ ku'sa' iya pʉra iyesi tʉwɨto' ipɨkɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pɨ', usoisaai amʉ' uya rɨ nin ari'po'pɨ'to' pe ta uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ inonkato' pe uya rɨ nin,” ta'pʉ Paire' uya. [</li>
      <li>To' Epoi Itɨ'pʉ Weyu Rʉ'pʉ a'tai, iteseru esi'pʉ Paire' uya tikin nɨ a'sisa' pe te'sen nonkato' pe iyesi Esuwerʉ amʉ' iwano' pe.]</li>
      <li>Tikin nɨ imaimu esii'ma to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Pʉse rɨ ka'pon atɨ' iwɨnɨ kon pa! Parapas nonkai'ma ina iwano' pe,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Parapas esi'pʉ a'sisa' pe, apʉne pʉra usewa'noman emapu'tɨsa' iya pɨ' Surusiran po mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon nɨrɨ wɨsa' iya pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Sises ɨnnonkapai tesi pɨ', Paire' uya kanan to' ekama'pokaa'pʉ.</li>
      <li>E'tane to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, “Kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'kɨ! Kurusu' pona ipokapɨ'kɨ!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Itosorʉwano ite'kwa pe to' auro'ka'pʉ iya, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe? Ɨ'rɨ ɨri ku'sa' pʉse rɨ ka'pon uya? Ɨ'rɨ rɨ ima'tato' ipɨkɨrɨ eposa' uya pʉra man. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', ikota'mato' pe ikupʉ uya, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ inonkato' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane eke pe to' ukɨ'pɨ'nʉnpɨtʉ'pʉ, tɨwɨ kurusu' pona ipokapɨtʉ nesii, tukai', mɨrɨpan kon nin si ena'pʉ imaimu entai.</li>
      <li>Paire' nin si ekoneka'pʉ mɨrɨ to' nesakʉ'pʉ ke to' repa pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon nonka'pʉ iya usewa'noman ku'sa' iya pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ka'pon nɨrɨ wɨsa' iya pɨ' a'sisa' rʉ'pʉ, to' nekama'po'pʉ, Sises nonkai'ma i'se to' e'to' ya'.</li>
      <li>To' uya arɨ koro'tau, ka'pon, Sairini pon Saiman itese', a'si'pʉ to' uya, Surusiran pona tʉutɨsen tʉmainarʉ awonsi'kɨ. Mɨrɨpan ena' kurusu' nonka'pʉ to' uya ato' pe iya Sises e'ma'pʉ pe.</li>
      <li>Tu'kan kon nɨ utɨ'pʉ Sises pɨkɨrɨ kurusu' pona soisa amʉ' uya ipokapɨ'to' ya'. Uri'sami'si amʉ' rɨ tʉuta'kwarʉkai' tʉukaransan iwenai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon winɨkʉi' Sises era'tɨ'pʉ, “Surusiran pon kon uri'sami'si amʉ', uwenai kakarantʉu; ɨwenai'nokon nɨ, ɨmunkɨ kon wenai rɨ akarantɨ', apʉne pʉra ɨsɨ rɨ e'ku'to' oton pɨ' ɨpɨ'nokon.</li>
      <li>Apʉne pʉra tato' oton to' uya iweyu e'seposa' a'tai, ‘Wakʉ ton kuru rɨ kamoro uri'sami'si amʉ' mʉre a'sinin nan pen, mʉre yen pe itewan e'sa' kon pen, mʉre na'su'ka'pʉ pen imanatʉ ton.’</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan tʉron kon uya tato' oton wʉ' ton pɨ', ‘Ina iwasa'kakɨ,’ i'kʉrʉ ton pɨ', ‘Ina iu'na'tɨkɨ,’ tato' oton to' uya.</li>
      <li>Serɨ kupʉ ka'pon amʉ' uya pe iyesi yau isenan pe yʉi esi koro'tau, ɨ'rɨ pe ken si iyesi mɨrɨ iyaipʉtasa' pe iyesi a'tai?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Asa'rɨ rɨ marɨ ɨri ku'nin nʉ'san ka'pon amʉ' enpa'ka'pʉ soisa amʉ' uya pata apai Sises pokon pe kurusu' pona to' pokapɨ'to' pe.</li>
      <li>Pata, Pu'pɨ Ɨ'pʉ rʉ'pʉ tato' eposa' to' uya a'tai, to' uya si kurusu' pona ipokapɨtʉ'pʉ ɨri ton pokon pe, tikin nɨ itenwo'netʉ winɨ, isakon ikamisi winɨ.</li>
      <li>Sises uya ta'pʉ, “Papai, to' pɨ' ɨsentu'makɨ, apʉne pʉra to' uya i'tu pʉra rɨ iyesi ɨri kupʉ tʉuya'nokon tukai',” ta'pʉ iya. Ipon nʉ'pʉ ta'nʉkʉ'pʉ to' uya te'wapiya'kapɨ'se.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' e'soto'pɨ'sa' esi'pʉ enpɨtʉ pɨ', Esuwerʉ amʉ' epuru ton uya Sises sapema'pʉ, “Tʉron kon sa'ne si pika'tɨ'pʉ iya, tɨwɨ si nepika'tɨi tiwano' pe, i'napai rɨ Kʉrai pe tesi yau, Papa Nanʉmʉ'pʉ pe,” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Te'neimapɨ'se soisa amʉ' usennaka'pʉ ipɨ', mɨrɨpan kon uya waain peneka ke iwo'pa'pʉ</li>
      <li>tai'ma, “Apʉne si Esuwerʉ amʉ' iwano' kin pe ɨwesi yau, ɨu'tɨkɨ kurusu' poi epika'tɨkɨ,” ta'pʉ to' uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan i'pai epoi tʉnmenuka'pʉ kon tʉsa' to' uya esi'pʉ: Pʉse rɨ si pʉse rɨ Esuwerʉ amʉ' iwano' kin, tawon.</li>
      <li>Ɨri ka'pon, ipokapɨ'sa' ipiyau uya rɨ isapema'pʉ, “Kʉrai pen nɨ pe' ɨmɨrɨ, epika'tɨkɨ, ina nɨrɨ ipika'tɨkɨ,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>E'tane isakon uya e'se'ne' pe eseremekʉ'pʉ, “Sises kasa rɨ pe' ama'tai'ma Papa nama auya pʉra iyesi?</li>
      <li>Iye'to' pe rɨ nin kurusu' pona to' uya upokapɨ'sa' kon serɨ ɨri ku'sa' wenai rɨ nin, e'tane pʉse rɨ uya ɨri ku'sa' pʉra rɨ iyesi, iwenai pʉra rɨ nin kurusu' pona to' uya ipokapɨ'sa' na'ne',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Sises, ɨyenu yau rʉ'kwɨ ukupʉi' kin pe ɨyenasa' a'tai,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Sises uya eikʉ'pʉ, “Ɨpɨ' ta uya serɨ, serɨ pe upiyau ɨwesi mɨrɨ wakʉ upata yau,” ta'pʉ Sises uya ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>12 a'kʉra' e'to' airɨ'ne rɨ, pata si ewarumamʉ'pʉ 3 a'kʉra' pʉ'kʉ pona rɨ,</li>
      <li>wʉi enu uya pata wei'tɨ pʉra iyesi'pʉ to' e'to' airɨ. Esuwerʉ amʉ' use'mato', ɨpʉremato' iwʉ' wapu ekaraka'pʉ a'sa'mʉyai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan Sises ukɨ'pɨ'nʉmʉ'pʉ, “Papai, ɨyena' si uya'kwarʉ sitʉyai'!” ta'pʉ iya. Serɨ ta tʉpo si, iyerikʉ'pʉ mɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Roman amʉ' soisaai ton epuru uya ensa' a'tai, Papa apurɨpɨtʉ'pʉ iya, “I'napai rɨ kuru rɨ ka'si, pʉse rɨ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ wa ipokena' e' pe,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ka'pon amʉ' iyamʉrasa' kon uya tanporo serɨ e'kupʉ ene'pʉ mɨrɨ, mɨrɨpan kon utɨ'pʉ ipan pe pokoi pe esii'ma.</li>
      <li>Tanporo kamoro Sises i'tunin nan e'soto'pɨ'sa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ te'ku'sen enpɨtʉ pɨ' ɨnnonsi'kɨ, uri'sami'si amʉ' rɨ esi'pʉ, iya'kɨrɨ iye'sa' kon nʉ'san Kiyarari poi.</li>
      <li>Moro ka'pon esi'pʉ Isose' itese', Konsʉrʉ pe te'sen, wakʉ mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ipoken te'sen awɨron,</li>
      <li>Papa e'to' esa' wannɨ pe e'seporo enupɨkɨrɨ te'sen. Kʉrɨ rɨ esi'pʉ asauro'se'na iyamʉrasa' kon tonpa pe rɨ, e'tane to' eseru pɨ', “Ewai',” tasa' iya pʉra iyesi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Itɨ'pʉ Roman amʉ' kopʉnaai, Paire' piya' Sises ekepu ekama'pose'na iu'na'tɨto' pe tʉuya. Mɨrɨpan pɨ', “Ewai',” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan mo'ka'pʉ iya, iwontɨ'pʉ iya epe'kena' pon renen tato' atʉ ke. Mɨrɨpan tʉrʉ'pʉ iya emenna' pe tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe ya'.</li>
      <li>Ekonekan weyu pe iyesi'pʉ, Sapa' nin si epiya'tɨkapʉ esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Uri'sami'si amʉ' Sises a'kɨrɨ iye'sa' kon nʉ'san Kiyarari poi utɨ'pʉ Isose' a'kɨrɨ. Mɨrɨpan kon uya Sises ekepu emaika ene'pʉ.</li>
      <li>To' enna'po'pʉ patatʉse' tʉuya'nokon ya'. Mɨrɨpan kon uya a'po'na' nan karapa konepɨtʉ'pʉ Sises ekepu karapaimato' tʉuya'nokon ike pe. To' nin si ereuta'pʉ mɨrɨ Sapa' weyu a'tai, Main uya tasa' na'ne' awɨrɨ.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Awanakʉi' kuru nin si suntaaka epiya'tɨ pe uri'sami'si amʉ' uya tʉnkoneka'pʉ kon a'po'na' nan arɨ esi'pʉ tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe pona.</li>
      <li>To' uya tɨ' e'tɨrinkasa', tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe apai eporo'pʉ,</li>
      <li>e'tane to' ewonsa' a'tai Sises ekepu pʉra iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ yau.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ' to' usenuminka koro'tau, ite'kwanau pʉra rɨ, asa'ron kon ka'pon amʉ' e'soto'ka'pʉ to' piyau, to' pon ton e'wei'tɨpɨtʉ'pʉ a'kwa pe, kamiri' kasa.</li>
      <li>Tetʉipɨtʉ kon pɨ' uri'sami'si amʉ' epeima'pʉ non pona, e'tane to' pɨ' ta'pʉ to' uya, “Ɨ'rɨto' pe eke' amʉ' koro'tau nurɨnan warinpa auya'nokon?</li>
      <li>Ipʉra man serɨ yau, iye'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ man. Ɨyenu kon yau iku'tɨ' inekama'pʉ ɨpiyau'nokon tesi koro'tau Kiyarari po,</li>
      <li>‘Ka'pon, Papa winon tʉto' oton ka'pon amʉ' uya tʉmakooikenan kon ena' to' uya ipokapɨ'to' pe kurusu' pona, e'tane iye'mʉ'sa'kato' oton itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai,’ tawon,” ta'pʉ to' iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ eta tʉuya'nokon a'tai, to' enu ya' si iyena'pʉ Sises maimu rʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Tenna'posa' kon a'tai, tɨ' akasa' uruwai' apai, 11 pan kon ipoitorʉ ton mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon ipoitorʉ ton pana'tɨ'pʉ to' uya tanporon nɨ iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ ke.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro uri'sami'si amʉ' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ, Meri Mataren, Isowana, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ Isens san, Meri rɨ marɨ itese', mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tʉron kon uri'sami'si amʉ' esi'pʉ to' a'kɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>E'tane uri'sami'si amʉ' uya tʉpana'tɨto' kon, apurɨ to' uya pʉra iyesi'pʉ, apʉne pʉra kasi poken iseta pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ rɨ e'tane, Pi'ta e'mʉ'sa'kasa' nin si eka'tumʉ'pʉ tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pona. Te'tɨmuikai' Sises ekepu ontɨto' ike pe isaai'pɨ'sa' rʉ'pʉ renen tato' atʉ ene'pʉ iya tʉpona rɨ. Mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ, “Ɨ'rɨ pe rɨ si iyesi'pʉ ko?” tai'ma.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ rɨ suntaaka e'sara'tɨ a'tai, asa'ron kon Sises poitorʉ ton utɨ esi'pʉ, eke iwa pata Emeyas tato' ka'pon amʉ' uya ya'. Serɨ pata esi'pʉ 7 mayirʉ e'to' airɨ rɨ Surusiran poi.</li>
      <li>Asaurokʉi'ma to' utɨ esi'pʉ tanporo iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ pɨ' Surusiran po.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ ton pɨ' usauro'nɨ pɨ' to' esi koro'tau, Sises uyee'pʉ a'ko pe to' piya', mɨrɨpan utɨ'pʉ to' a'kɨrɨ,</li>
      <li>e'tane Papa uya to' uya ito'ka'nʉkʉ namai' Sises ku'sa' esi'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon ekama'po'pʉ Sises uya, “Ɨ'rɨ pɨ' asaurokʉi'ma ɨutɨ kon?” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'. Mɨrɨpan kon e'takʉ'kasa' umaintapɨtʉ'pʉ,</li>
      <li>mɨrɨpan isakon Kiriyo'pas itese' uya ta'pʉ Sises pɨ', “Ɨmɨrɨ rɨken na'kɨ si nai serɨ ton, Surusiran po iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ i'tunin pe pʉra,” ta'pʉ ipɨ'.</li>
      <li>“Ɨ'rɨ ton si e'kupʉ'pʉ?” ta'pʉ nin si Sises uya mɨrɨ ipɨ'. “Mɨ ton sa'ne, Sises, Nasare' pon pɨ' iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ. Pu'kena' pe sa'ne iyesi tukai', Papa ni'tunʉ, ka'pon amʉ' rɨ nɨrɨ ni'tunʉ, meruntɨ pe tʉusauro'sen, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ ɨ'rɨ rɨ ku'nin meruntɨ pe.</li>
      <li>Use'man nɨto' tʉrawasomanin nan epuru ton eke ton kuru, mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ uyepuru kon amʉ' uya itʉrʉ'pʉ Roman amʉ' kopʉnaai ena' to' uya iwɨto' pe iku'to' pe iya. Mɨrɨpan pokapɨ'sa' to' uya kurusu' pona erikʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Ina sa'ne si Esuwerʉ amʉ' mo'ka iya ina eyaton non enapai tukai' ina e'ku'sa' e'tane. Mɨrɨ rɨken pe ekama tane, serɨ si osorʉwau wʉi iko'mankapʉ to' uya iwɨnɨ'pʉ si'kɨrɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pona ina koro'tau te'san uri'sami'si amʉ' uya ina ewansiukapɨ'an ko. Awanakʉi' kuru to' utɨ'pʉ tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe pona, e'tane itekepu pʉra iyesi'pʉ mɨrɨ yau. Mɨrɨpan kon uye'sa' uya ina pana'tɨ'pʉ inserʉ amʉ' ene'pʉ tʉuya'nokon tukai'. Mɨrɨpan kon uya, ‘Sises e'mʉ'sa'ka'pʉ man,’ ta'pʉ to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan ina tonpa ton kanan utɨkaa'pʉ tɨ' akasa' uruwai' pe pona, mɨrɨpan kon uya si eporo'pʉ uri'sami'si amʉ' uya ekama'pʉ kasa rɨ, Sises ene'pʉ to' uya pen nɨ kanan,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan a'tai, Sises uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Nai pan kon ɨmɨrɨ'nokon iya'kwarʉ pʉnon kon nɨ, apurɨ auya'nokon pʉra kuru rɨ iyesi pu'kena' amʉ' nekama'pʉ te'ku'ton tukai'.</li>
      <li>Papa uya rɨ sa'ne iku'sa' esi'pʉ mɨrɨ ko pʉse rɨ tʉnanʉmʉ'pʉ ekota'mato' pe rɨ. Mɨrɨpan i'mʉ'sa'kasa' tʉuya e'to' pe tapurɨpɨ'sen pe Epʉn po,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan uya to' pɨ' ekama'pʉ tʉpɨ' itekare usauro'sa' Mosi' nʉmenuka'pʉ si'kɨrɨ te'sara'tɨi', siya rɨ pu'kena' amʉ' nʉmenuka'pʉ rɨ tʉpɨ'.</li>
      <li>To' uya si a'ko pe eke iwa pata epokapʉ esi'pʉ mɨrɨ tʉutɨto' kon ya', e'tane Sises e'kupʉ'pʉ to' entawon ya' parɨ tʉutɨ pe itese'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ' ta'pʉ to' uya, “Pata itʉkɨ ina piyau, apʉne pʉra pata newarumanka'an,” ta'pʉ to' uya. Mɨrɨpan kon piya' iyewomʉ'pʉ.</li>
      <li>Iyereuta'pʉ to' pokon pe enta'nase'na, mɨrɨpan uya tenki ta pe Papa pɨ' pʉreti anʉmʉ'pʉ, i'kwɨtʉ'pʉ iya, mɨrɨpan tʉrʉ'pʉ iya to' ena'. Mɨrɨ a'tai, Papa uya to' enu a'koka'pʉ, mɨrɨpan to'ka'nʉkʉ'pʉ to' uya, mɨrɨpan kon enu apai'ka'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya ta'pʉ, “Uyewan kon sa'ne a'pɨ'pɨtʉi ko asanta tau uyauro'ka iya 'nokon koro'tau pu'kena' amʉ' nekama'pʉ iye'menukasa' itekare pɨ',” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon e'mʉ'sa'kasa' utɨ'pʉ oko pe pʉra rɨ, Surusiran pona. Mɨrɨ yau, 11 pan kon Sises poitorʉ ton amʉrasa' eporo'pʉ to' uya tʉron kon ipoitorʉ ton pokon pe.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya pʉsamoro asa'ron kon pɨ' ta'pʉ, “I'napairɨ rɨ kenʉ' Sises e'mʉ'sa'kasa' man! Mɨrɨpan ene'pʉ Pi'ta uya!” ta'pʉ to' uya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pʉsamoro asa'ron kon uya Emeas e'ma tau iye'ku'sa' rʉ'pʉ ekama'pʉ kanan to' pɨ', ito'ka'nʉkʉ'pʉ tʉuya'nokon pʉreti i'kwɨtʉ iya a'tai.</li>
      <li>Pʉsamoro rɨ si usaurokʉ koro'tau mɨrɨ pɨ', Sises e'soto'ka'pʉ to' koro'ta'. Mɨrɨpan uya ta'pʉ to' pɨ', “Miyarɨ'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Ipan pe to' etʉipɨtʉ'pʉ, a'kwarʉ'pʉ ensa' tʉuya'nokon pe tekamai'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Tetʉipɨ'se pʉra e'tɨ', tʉkasimai' pʉra, e'mʉ'sa'kasa' apurɨtɨ',</li>
      <li>apʉne upokapɨtʉ'pʉ iyɨ rʉ'pʉ entɨ', uyemiyatʉ pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ u'ta pɨ'. Urɨ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ, uya'kwarʉ'pʉ ensa' auya'nokon pen, uya'pɨ'tɨ', urɨ rɨ kʉrɨ rɨ. Urɨ kasa pe' tʉpun ke a'kwarʉ'pʉ esi pe ekama auya'nokon,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ ta tʉuya a'tai, tʉpokapɨtʉ'pʉ ɨ rʉ'pʉ enpoika'pʉ iya mɨrɨ to' ena'.</li>
      <li>Pori' pe kuru tesi kon ke, “I'napai rɨ se esi pen nɨ serɨ?” ta'pʉ to' uya. Mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' ta'pʉ iya, “Kiyari pe' moro nai enta'nan nɨto' ipɨ'?” ta'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya irepa'pʉ akuse pe ikanpʉ'tɨsa' moro' ke.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan pɨ' iyenta'na'pʉ to' enu airɨ.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon pɨ' ta'pʉ Sises uya, “Ɨ'koro'tau'nokon sa'ne esi a'tai, erikʉ rawɨrɨ, sekamatai ɨpɨ'nokon ko tanporon nɨ Mosi' Maimu, pu'kena' amʉ' Maimu rɨ, Eren yau'ne isauro'sa' na'ne' upɨ' uta'ku'tɨto' pe iyesi ukatai ko,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon uya tʉpɨ' iye'menukasa' itekare to'ka'nʉ'to' pe to' uya ikupʉ'pʉ,</li>
      <li>To' pɨ' ekama'pʉ iya, “Serɨ serɨ iye'menukasa' rʉ'pʉ: Kʉrai uya e'ne' moronkato' oton, mɨrɨpan eri'to' oton, te'mʉ'sa'ka ton pe itosorʉwano wʉi a'tai.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ tanporon kon tʉpataron kon pɨ' itekare usekamato' oton itese' yau, makoi apai era'tɨn nɨto' pɨ' mɨrɨ awonsi'kɨ makoi pɨ' usentu'man nɨto' pɨ', Surusiran po te'sara'tɨi'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', entantɨ' tʉron kon kanan ipana'tɨtantɨ' ɨnene'pʉ kon pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Serɨ pe iwa rɨ, ukʉipʉnʉ usaurokʉ'pʉ ennoko uya ta'pʉ rʉ'pʉ iya'kwarʉ ennoko uya mɨrɨ ɨpiya'nokon. Mɨrɨ pe iyesi pɨ', serɨ yau Surusiran po e'tɨ' Papa winon ɨmeruntɨrʉ kon eporo auya'nokon pʉ'kʉ pona,” ta'pʉ iya to' pɨ'.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨ a'tai, Sises uya to' arɨ'pʉ Surusiran poi a'ko pe rɨ pata Pe'tani piya'. To' uya eposa' a'tai, temiyatʉ tanʉnse to' pʉrema'pʉ iya.</li>
      <li>To' pʉrema pɨ' iyesi koro'tau, to' nɨmɨ'pʉ iya, itanʉmʉ'pʉ Epʉn pona.</li>
      <li>Ipoitorʉ ton e'sekunka'pʉ apurɨpɨ'se'na. Mɨrɨpan kon enna'po'pʉ ipan pe rɨ pori' pe esii'ma Surusiran pona.</li>
      <li>Mɨrɨpan kon esi'pʉ Papa apurɨpɨtʉ pɨ', inke rɨ wʉi kaisa rɨ use'man nɨto', ɨpʉreman nɨto' iwʉ' pʉ'kʉ tau.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
</ol>
